Japanese Cabinet Decision: Abolish Jurisdictional Rights in Manchukuo; Ministry of Foreign Affairs Issues Statement

(Tokyo) The abolition of extraterritorial rights in "Manchukuo" and the transfer of administrative rights over the South Manchuria Railway (SMR) attached areas have been decided by the Cabinet today. The details are as follows:

The abolition of the extraterritorial rights of the Empire in Manchuria and the administrative rights over the SMR attached areas will be studied by relevant officials based on the following principles, with the aim of implementation as soon as possible: (1) Regarding the extraterritorial rights of the Empire in "Manchukuo," the systems implemented in "Manchukuo" in accordance with the spirit of treaties should be adapted, taking into consideration the drastic changes in the lives of imperial subjects residing in Manchuria, further ensuring the peaceful residence and development of virtuous imperial subjects in "Manchukuo," and the smooth implementation of imperial national policy in Manchuria. In particular, gradual abolition should be considered. (2) The SMR attached lands should still be maintained by Japan, but the imperial administrative rights exercised in those lands should be adjusted or transferred in accordance with the systems implemented in "Manchukuo," considering the connection with the abolition of jurisdictional rights, and in line with the pace of gradual abolition of extraterritorial rights, considering the nature of each item. (9th, Domei News Agency)

(Tokyo) The Empire's government's policy on the abolition of jurisdictional rights in Manchuria and the transfer of administrative rights over the SMR attached areas was decided at the Cabinet meeting on the 9th. Therefore, the Ministry of Foreign Affairs issued a statement in the form of an official statement, expressing the intention to transfer administrative rights gradually in accordance with the development and system improvement of "Manchukuo," and to support the completion of the "Manchukuo" state. The statement from the Ministry of Foreign Affairs is as follows:

(1) The basic principle of the Empire's policy toward "Manchukuo" has been detailed in the Japan-Manchukuo Protocol and the Imperial Edict on withdrawing from the League of Nations, ensuring that "Manchukuo" maintains an inseparable relationship with the Empire, achieving sound development as an independent nation, thereby ensuring the stability of East Asia, and declaring the great righteousness of the Empire's national policy both domestically and abroad. (2) However, the extraterritorial rights that the Empire has enjoyed in Manchuria for many years were an important condition for the development of Manchuria before the establishment of "Manchukuo," but this has now lost its importance. At the same time, in order to achieve the sound development of "Manchukuo," promote genuine harmony between Japan and "Manchukuo," ensure the full development of the Japanese people in "Manchukuo," and further strengthen the friendly and permanent inseparable relationship between Japan and "Manchukuo," it is necessary to abolish those rights. Therefore, the administrative rights exercised under treaties in the SMR attached areas must also be adjusted or transferred in accordance with the new situation after the establishment of "Manchukuo," based on the necessity of abolishing extraterritorial rights. The Empire's government has decided on the outline at the Cabinet meeting on the 9th and hopes to implement it step by step. (A) Special consideration should be given to ensuring that the lives of imperial subjects in Manchuria do not undergo drastic changes, and to ensuring the peaceful residence and development of imperial subjects, and to ensuring that the Empire's national policy can be implemented smoothly. Therefore, gradual abolition will be implemented. (B) The adjustment and transfer of administrative rights over the SMR attached areas should be consistent with the gradual abolition of extraterritorial rights. It should also be mentioned that it is completely unrelated to the lease rights of the Kwantung Leased Territory. (9th, Domei News Agency)

Further French Financial Plan: Revive Economy, Reduce Prices; Continued Promulgation of 83 Substitute Laws; Undertake Public Works to Absorb Unemployment; Reduce Land Tax, Encourage Exports, Benefit Farmers and Workers

(Paris) Last night, the French government issued 83 decrees. The new laws are divided into four categories: (1) protecting investors; (2) restoring the economy, with undertaking public works as an urgent task; (3) reducing the cost of living, which is the result of agreements between the government and food merchants; (4) revising the laws promulgated in the decree of July 17. Prime Minister Laval told reporters that the July 17 decree had restored the balance of the budget and preserved the franc. This decree can help restore the economy, which is the government's main goal. At the same time, the government will complete its work and implement plans to reduce certain consumer prices and equalize the burdens and sacrifices of the people. The government will use 100,000 francs to build public works such as roads and flood control, in order to settle unemployed people. This plan will be financed by borrowing. The government will also establish a central committee to prevent unemployment in northern France, which will protect French workers by cracking down on overtime work and restricting foreign workers. The government will soon issue decrees to protect investors, prevent fraud, improve bankruptcy laws, and increase the responsibility of company directors. Import quotas will be eliminated for the same industrial products, but not for agricultural products. At the same time, state governors will have the power to set the maximum retail price of meat, and those who violate it will be punished. Farmers' land rents will be reduced by one-tenth, and fertilizer prices will also be reduced. The financial crisis has now passed, and the government will continue to work hard without any retreat, and will fulfill its responsibilities. If the people respond to this effort in a disciplined manner, the revival of economic undertakings will be possible tomorrow. At the same time, the interest rate on treasury bonds has been reduced from 3.5% to 3%. (9th, Reuters)

(Paris) Yesterday, the Council of State held a meeting to draft several substitute legal orders in the second batch (the first batch of decrees reducing government spending was announced on July 17 of this year) to prepare for economic recovery. These orders are divided into several categories, one of which focuses particularly on preventing unemployment. The previously planned large-scale public works program, although postponed for some reason, has now been decided to start immediately throughout the country. The cost will be temporarily limited to 100 million francs. The funds saved by each province and town due to the implementation of reduced government spending will be used to carry out local projects. The government has also decided to establish a central committee to prevent unemployment to oversee its completion. The second is to protect savings undertakings, and to prescribe strict punishment measures for those who violate credit and defraud property in the name of conducting savings. The third is to abolish the method of limiting the import quotas of certain goods in order to encourage exports. The fourth is to adjust the meat market and reduce retail prices. The fifth is to reform the procedures that hinder economic recovery, so that they tend to be simple. That is, the procedure for revising various commercial contracts should be simplified, the method of penalizing 10% of the unpaid tax should be cancelled, and the cost of paying taxes should be reduced. (9th, Havas)

(Rome) An Italian plane flying from Rome to Massawa in Eritrea, Africa, went missing on Wednesday morning after leaving Cairo. Commercial Dispute Resolved: Poland and Danzig Reach Agreement; Poland Agrees to Abolish Tariff Law; Danzig Abandons Retaliatory Measures

Danzig: The governments of Danzig and Poland signed an agreement here this afternoon stipulating that the Polish government will abolish the tariff law promulgated on July 17. All import taxes should be paid at Polish customs thereafter. At the same time, Danzig withdrew its retaliatory plan, stipulating that certain goods can be transported and sold in Danzig duty-free. The detailed measures will be discussed after the end of this negotiation in order to resolve all outstanding issues between Danzig and Poland. (8th, National News)

Warsaw: The Free City of Danzig and Poland have once again reached a compromise to resolve the commercial war. Poland had previously raised tariffs to restrict the import of Danzig goods. Danzig then adopted a retaliatory plan to turn Danzig into a free port to benefit Germany. Now, after negotiations between the two parties, Danzig has agreed to cancel the temporary order to open the border and allow German goods to enter duty-free. At the same time, Poland has also agreed that goods transported from Danzig to Poland will be collected by Danzig customs, but the tariffs paid should be in Polish currency, not Danzig currency. (9th, Reuters)

Warsaw: The Polish government has repeatedly protested and clashed with Danzig because the Free City of Danzig has allowed certain goods to be imported into Danzig duty-free. The dispute was resolved today. Because Polish Foreign Minister Beck was on his way to Finland via the port of Gdynia, Danzig Free City Senate Speaker Glaysett went to the port today to hold a meeting with Polish Foreign Minister Beck. A protocol was signed by both parties stipulating that the Free City of Danzig would revoke the order issued on August 1 to establish a customs office in the Free City to collect taxes. From then on, goods imported into Danzig would be subject to tariffs in Polish currency "Złoty" in order to protect the Polish economy and prevent it from being affected by the devaluation of Danzig currency. As for the Polish side, the protocol stipulated that the order issued on July 18 should be revoked. This order stipulated that all goods imported into Poland from Danzig must be subject to tariffs within Poland (after that, taxes can be paid within Danzig). In addition, the Polish government promised not to take any retaliatory measures against Danzig's measures to prohibit the export of currency. In addition, the two sides will start negotiations on currency issues within days to seek a solution. (8th, Havas)

The various declarations made by its leaders and members are sufficient to show opposition to or hostility towards the government. The orders recently issued by the government authorities to the group have also been met with contempt, as in the past. As of now, those who have joined the Steel Helmet League, if they have never participated in the front-line industry, are either Marxists or members of other political parties who oppose the government. Therefore, the Steel Helmet League has in fact become the tail of the reactionaries. For the sake of national security, the branches of the group in Berlin, Brandenburg, Pomerania, and Austria are hereby dissolved. (8th, National News)

Anti-Jewish and Anti-Christian Activities Still Not Stopped

(Munich) Munich began a campaign to cleanse the Jewish people from Bavaria's summer resorts today. Bavarian Interior Minister Wagner, who is also the district leader of the National Socialist Party in Bavaria, sent a telegram of congratulations to the city of Bad Toelz for having completely expelled all Jewish people, and expressed the wish that the entire Bavarian mountain region could follow suit. At the same time, a priest from a monastery near Koblenz was arrested for allegedly tearing down posters of the National Socialist Party and smearing the posters with black ink. (9th, Reuters)

Landslide in the Philippines Buries a Small Village Completely; Severe Flooding in North-Central Region

(Manila) Today, the largest landslide in the history of the Philippines occurred in Northern Luzon, near the town of Bokod, 175 miles north of here. The landslide completely buried a small village, with 50 residents inside. Simultaneously, due to floods in Central and Northern Luzon, a total of 202 people have died, and thousands are homeless. Public works have suffered extensive damage, and the losses to crops are inestimable. (Reuters, 9th)

Shanghai Mysterious Westerner Case: Hubei High Court Has Filed Charges Against Joseph Walton and Seven Others for Jointly Endangering the Republic of China; Yuan Shu Transferred to Hubei Rehabilitation Institute

Wuchang Correspondence: Joseph Walton, the mysterious Westerner from Shanghai, was arrested in Shanghai by the Songhu Garrison Headquarters for endangering the Republic of China. Subsequently, several other key figures involved in the case were arrested and transferred by the Military Affairs Commission's Executive Office to the Hubei High Court for interrogation. Except for Yuan Shu, whose case has already been adjudicated and who has been transferred to the Rehabilitation Institute, Joseph Walton, Huang Weiyou (female), Lu Haifang (male), Wang Moqing, Hu Kelin, Chen Wenjie, and Yu Ruiyuan, a total of seven individuals, have now had their cases investigated by High Court Prosecutor Shi Zhenxiang. Based on the Emergency Law for Punishing Offenses Against the Republic of China, a public prosecution has been filed. This case has attracted attention both domestically and internationally. The indictment is recorded below:

Names of the Accused

Joseph Walton, male, 39 years old, Westerner, nationality unknown, residing in Shanghai. Huang Weiyou, female, 23 years old, from Hunan, graduate student at Jiaotong University, residing at 16 Huihai Road, Nanjing. Lu Haifang (also known as Wu Shenru), male, 29 years old, from Hunan, graduate of Beiping Normal University, residing on Albert Road, Shanghai. Wang Moqing (also known as Wang Hanmin), 22 years old, from Shandong, graduate of Qufu Normal School, residing at 925 Avenue Joffre, Shanghai. Hu Kelin, male, 24 years old, from Sichuan, student, residing on Xinzha Road, Shanghai. Chen Wenjie, male, 23 years old, from Jiangsu, graduate of Cheng Lie Physical Education School, residing at 51 W鹊 Bridge Lane, Suzhou. Yu Ruiyuan, male, 36 years old, from Zhejiang, graduate of Hangzhou Zhijiang University, residing in Haining. The above-listed defendants, in a case of endangering the Republic of China, have been investigated, and it is deemed that a public prosecution should be filed. The facts of the crime, the evidence, and the articles of law violated are listed below.

Facts of the Crime

Defendant Joseph Walton, under the direction of the Third International's GPU, hid in Shanghai, colluding with fugitive Communist Party members Liu Suiyuan and Xiao Bingshi, as well as defendants Lu Haifang and Huang Weiyou, to spy on China's political and military secrets. Liu Suiyuan, working as a colonel-level regulations specialist in the Fifth Division of the Wuchang Executive Office, used his position to collect information about the aforementioned matters and supplied it to the traitors through Huang Weiyou and Lu Haifang. On April 19 of this year, Joseph Walton sent a secret letter in German to Liu Suiyuan. This letter was given by Joseph Walton to Lu Haifang, who in turn gave it to Lu Dubu (also known as Qian Zhenhua) to take to Hankou and deliver to Liu Suiyuan. Lu Dubu was arrested upon arrival in Hankou, and the aforementioned letter was found on his person. On April 27, Liu Suiyuan, expecting Qian Zhenhua to arrive in Hankou as agreed, wired Huang Weiyou to inquire. Huang Weiyou informed Lu Haifang and Joseph Walton. Joseph Walton, realizing that the matter had been discovered, immediately ordered Huang Weiyou to fly to Hankou, secretly instructing Liu Suiyuan to leave his post immediately and providing 351 yuan for his escape. This occurred on April 29. After Liu Suiyuan fled, his wife, Zeng Zhaorong, also left. On May 5, they arrived in Shanghai and stayed at the Dongya Hotel. Lu Haifang and Huang Weiyou visited them successively. The Songhu Garrison Headquarters' investigation team, in conjunction with the Shanghai Municipal Police, tracked them down. Later, Lu Haifang left the hotel and hired a car. The detectives, believing him to be Liu Suiyuan, who they were ordered to arrest, shouted "Mr. Liu." Lu Haifang, realizing he was being pursued, identified himself as Lu Haifang and confessed to joining the Communist Party. Within fifteen minutes of his arrest, he led the detectives to the pre-arranged meeting place with Joseph Walton and identified Joseph Walton for arrest. The detectives found on Joseph Walton's person several pieces of evidence, including English expense accounts for the organization from April to May 2. Lu Haifang then exposed his co-conspirators Wang Moqing and Hu Kelin, who had joined the organization and transmitted secret documents, as well as Yu Ruiyuan, who had served as a translator. They were also arrested. An English warning letter from Joseph Walton was found in Huang Weiyou's room at Jiaotong University. Because Liu Suiyuan's actions were exposed, he and his wife, Zeng Zhaorong, fled from Shanghai to Chen Wenjie's home in Suzhou. When the detectives went to arrest them, Liu Suiyuan and his wife had already fled upon hearing the news, so Chen Wenjie was arrested and sent to this court for investigation.

Evidence of the Crime and Articles of Law Violated

The facts of the crime in this case are as described above. The evidence presented that is sufficient to prove the crimes of the defendants is described as follows:

(1) Regarding the portion of Joseph Walton: The defendant stubbornly refuses to confess to the facts of the crime, and even conceals his name and nationality, refusing to reveal them. This shows his cunning nature. However, although the defendant stubbornly refuses to admit guilt, the important evidence of his crime is as follows: (A) The defendant's letter in German to Liu Suiyuan. The letter states, "Not only should you pay attention to positive news regarding military issues, but also to political issues, especially the situation presented by Sichuan," and instructs him to spy on issues relating to Sichuan and Xinjiang. The end of the letter gives instructions regarding Liu Suiyuan's communication techniques, intending to maintain secrecy and avoid revealing weaknesses. The defendant is proficient in English, French, German, and Russian, with German being his best (see the defendant's statement on July 2). Liu Suiyuan studied in Germany for many years and is also well-versed in German. Therefore, the defendant's letters to Liu Suiyuan were always in German. The defendant signed the letter "Lorenz" (the warning letter to Huang Weiyou was signed "Roar") and had it transmitted through Lu Haifang and Lu Dubu. Not only did Lu Dubu confess when he was arrested in Hankou, but Lu Haifang also identified him definitively during their confrontation in court. (B) English expense accounts found on the defendant's person. These English expense accounts are records of Lu Haifang's income and expenses from April to May 2 of this year, which he personally reported to the defendant. Lu Haifang explained each item on the expense accounts, including codes such as "No. 204," which refers to the wanted criminal Liu Suiyuan; "No. 207," which refers to Chen Shaohan, a colonel staff officer of the Third Army; "Nanjing Woman," which refers to Huang Weiyou; and "Banker's Daughter," which refers to Jiang Junyu. Also found was a small envelope containing four items of English notes: 1. A letter about an appointment with a famous woman; 2. Accounts for April to May 2; 3. A letter from No. 204; 4. The address of a Sichuan person. The "famous woman" refers to the famous woman listed in the English expense accounts as receiving a silver dollar payment. "Accounts for April to May 1" refers to the aforementioned English expense accounts. "No. 204" refers to Liu Suiyuan, who is listed as No. 204 in the English expense accounts. "Sichuan Person" refers to Hu Kelin, who is listed in the English expense accounts as a Sichuan person. This note can be confirmed by the English expense accounts. The defendant's crime can be seen from this one aspect. In addition, there was an English typed letter regarding the suppression of bandits in Guizhou, Sichuan, Xiangxi, and Exi, and a Russian typed letter dated March 27 of this year, signed "Yarting," stating, "We are not completely satisfied with Pan Fei'er. He is often deceived by information peddlers, and the sources of the materials collected by the information peddlers are mostly hearsay and completely incorrect." These are clearly related to spying on military and political secrets. Other evidence, such as Lu Haifang's statement about the important mailbox at 2018, is sufficient ironclad proof of the defendant's crime. (C) The defendant's English warning letter to Huang Weiyou. This letter was given by the defendant to Lu Haifang to be delivered to Huang Weiyou on April 12 of this year. The contents promote the importance of the proletarian revolution, the strict organization of the party, and encourages her to embrace the determination to sacrifice and fight to become a powerful soldier. This letter was found by the Songhu Garrison Headquarters in Huang Weiyou's room and was confirmed by Huang Weiyou and Lu Haifang. Based on the above evidence, the defendant Joseph Walton directed Liu Suiyuan, Chen Shaohan, and Communist Party members Lu Haifang, Huang Weiyou, and other high-ranking officials of the Chinese Bandit Suppression Organization to spy on political and military secrets and supply them to traitors, which constitutes a violation of Article 5, Section 2 of the Emergency Law for Punishing Offenses Against the Republic of China.

(2) Regarding the portion of Huang Weiyou: The defendant joined the Communist Youth League in 1926. In 1927, she worked in the Women's Department of Nanxian County, Hunan. In September of last year, she was introduced by Liu Suiyuan to Xiao Bingshi, and then by Xiao Bingshi to Joseph Walton, to serve as a translator of various military and political news and to handle transportation, under the direct command of Joseph Walton. When Liu Suiyuan was a compiler in the Ministry of Interior, the materials he supplied to the Communist Party were transmitted by the defendant. She also used her classmate Jiang Junyu as an intelligence receiving agency. When Liu Suiyuan's case was exposed, she flew from Shanghai to Hankou to urge Liu to flee quickly to avoid arrest. Shortly after, Liu's wife, Zeng Zhaorong, fled to Shanghai. The defendant hid Zeng Zhaorong from the Dongya Hotel to another place. All of these facts have been confessed by the defendant and confirmed by the English warning letter from Joseph Walton found in her room by the Songhu Garrison Headquarters, as well as the "Report of the Central Executive Committee and the People's Committee of the Pseudo-Chinese Soviet Republic on the Second National Soviet Congress" and various reactionary publications. In the English expense accounts found on Joseph Walton's person, items 18, 25, and 26 list payments of silver dollars to a "Nanjing Woman," which is the defendant's code name. Thus, her joining the organization and engaging in work is very clear. Her actions, according to Article 11, Article 28, Article 56 of the Criminal Law, constitute a violation of Article 5, Section 2 of the Emergency Law for Punishing Offenses Against the Republic of China.

(3) Regarding the portion of Lu Haifang: The defendant joined the Communist Party organization in 1927 while working in the Political Department of the 11th Army. Around July of last year, he met Xiao Bingshi through the introduction of Zhang Fangzhi. From then on, he became close to Joseph Walton and was responsible for translating and transmitting various military and political secrets. Since December of last year, the defendant has been responsible for handling the payment of funds for the organization. The importance of his work is self-evident. His actions constitute a violation of Article 5, Section 2 of the Emergency Law for Punishing Offenses Against the Republic of China. However, when the detectives tracked and arrested him at the Dongya Hotel on May 5 of this year, they thought the defendant was the wanted criminal Liu Suiyuan and did not know that he was Lu Haifang, nor did they know who Lu Haifang was. They were even more unaware of whether he had a significant relationship with the case or any criminal behavior. However, the defendant resolutely surrendered himself, admitted that he was Lu Haifang, and clearly stated the criminal facts of the past and his relationship with the case. He immediately led the detectives to Fuxu Road to arrest the main criminal Joseph Walton and several other co-conspirators to show his sincerity in surrendering. As a result, a large number of reactionary documents and various evidence were seized. The breakthrough of the entire case was due to the defendant's change of heart. This situation is in accordance with the provisions of Article 3 of the Implementing Regulations of the Emergency Law for Punishing Offenses Against the Republic of China and Article 3 of the Communist Self-Surrender Law.

(4) Regarding the portions of Wang Moqing and Hu Kelin: Wang Moqing, also known as Wang Hanmin, was introduced to Lu Haifang by Yang Zhuo. His task was to make contacts, collect materials, and serve as a courier for transmitting secret documents, i.e., the "Second Radio Operator" referred to in items 7, 9, 21, 48, and 49 of the English expense accounts. According to the defendant's confession, "I went to Hankou once in March of this year to deliver a letter from Lu Haifang to Liu Suiyuan. Liu also wrote a reply and gave it to me to take to Lu Haifang. I know Hu Kelin, who was also introduced by Lu Haifang. He (referring to Hu Kelin) cut out newspaper clippings about military news and sent them to Lu Haifang, three times a week. Monthly living expenses were always less than 45 yuan and were not fixed" (see the investigation record of July 29 of this year). The defendant Hu Kelin is the "Sichuan Person" listed in the English expense accounts as receiving 80 yuan for four months of living expenses. According to the defendant's confession, "I met Lu Haifang in February of this year through the introduction of Ren Yue. When Mr. Ren introduced us, he said that he had a friend who wanted to study politics and economics and asked me to collect materials for him and sometimes transmit letters. The materials I collected concerned politics, namely, the Sino-Japanese problem, the problem between the Central Government and the Southwest. Regarding military affairs, I collected important news about bandit suppression. The materials were originally sent to Mr. Wu (i.e., Lu Haifang), but later they were sent to Mr. Ye, i.e., this Mr. Wang (referring to Wang Moqing)" (see the investigation record of July 29 of this year). When questioned, Lu Haifang also stated that Wang Moqing and Hu Kelin were responsible for transmitting military and political secrets. The defendants Wang Moqing and Hu Kelin, according to Article 11, Article 28, and Article 56 of the Criminal Law, jointly committed the crime of violating Article 5, Section 2 of the Emergency Law for Punishing Offenses Against the Republic of China.

(5) Regarding the portion of Yu Ruiyuan: The defendant and the Communist Xiao Bingshi were classmates at Zhijiang University in Hangzhou. Through the introduction of Xiao Bingshi, he met Lu Haifang and was responsible for translating materials, the sources of which were magazines, newspapers, printed matter, etc. The content was military and political news. His monthly salary was 100 yuan. From January to early April, he received a total of 300 yuan. According to the defendant's confession, in early April, he felt it was dangerous and abandoned it, returning to his position as director of registration at Shanghai University. The defendant served as a translator for a long time and was friendly with the wanted Communist criminal Xiao Bingshi. It is difficult to deny that he was unaware of the organization's spying on military and political secrets and to disclaim responsibility. His actions, according to Article 11 and Article 30 of the Criminal Law, constitute a violation of Article 5, Section 2 of the Emergency Law for Punishing Offenses Against the Republic of China. However, according to Lu Haifang's statement, "Yu Ruiyuan has no political connections and was completely forced by circumstances" (see the investigation record of July 30 of this year). Considering the reasons for his crime, there are still grounds for leniency.

(6) Regarding the portion of Chen Wenjie: The defendant's brother, Chen Wenlu, brought the wanted criminal Liu Suiyuan and his wife, Zeng Zhaorong, to his home in mid-May of this year and hid them. Liu Suiyuan, fearing being discovered due to the presence of many detectives, fled to Taiyuan with Chen Wenlu after three days. His wife, Zeng Zhaorong, hid in the defendant's home for more than ten days before escaping when detectives came to arrest her. During that time, Chen Wenlu asked Chen Wenjie to exchange 800 yuan of remittance for Liu Suiyuan, which the defendant secured through a guarantor. Later, Zeng Zhaorong planned to escape from Suzhou to Jinan, and Chen Wenjie was given 170 silver yuan by Chen Qi'ing to buy train tickets to Jinan for both of them. The defendant was arrested while about to purchase the tickets. From various sources, it is clear that the defendant knew that Liu Suiyuan and his wife had committed a crime and were trying to escape. Knowing that they were traitors, he hid them without reporting them, which constitutes a violation of Article 4 of the Emergency Law for Punishing Offenses Against the Republic of China.

In conclusion, combining Article 1 of the Implementing Regulations of the Emergency Law for Punishing Offenses Against the Republic of China, Article 230, Section 1, and Article 243 of the Criminal Procedure Law, a public prosecution is filed. Respectfully submitted to the Criminal Division of this Court. Prosecutor Shi Zhenxiang (sealed), (8th)

Southern Fujian Hurricane Rain: Quanzhou's Flood Catastrophe

—Unprecedented in Hundreds of Years—

Xiamen Dispatch: The severe storm and heavy rain on July 23rd caused significant damage in the Zhangzhou, Quanzhou, and Yongchun areas. Transportation was fully restored on the 27th. However, only three days later, a second hurricane landed in the Xiamen, Zhangzhou, and Quanzhou areas on the morning of the 30th, accompanied by heavy rain, continuing for two days and nights. As of the 1st of this month, the rain was still intermittent. The intensity and duration of the storm were far greater than the first one. On the 30th, transportation between Xiamen and Zhangzhou, Quanzhou, was again completely cut off. Telegraph and telephone lines were all disrupted. Telephone lines between Zhangzhou and Xiamen were restored on the night of the 30th. On the 2nd, the wind subsided, and ships arrived in Quanzhou, but land transportation remained disrupted until the 3rd.

In Quanzhou, from 2:00 AM on the 30th, hurricane-force winds and torrential rain continued throughout the day. In the evening, flash floods erupted in the east and west streams of Nanan, rushing towards Quanzhou city. The sea tide was also driven into the harbor by the hurricane, causing the water to be unable to drain. The mountain torrents poured into the city, causing a severe flood disaster. Eighty percent of the entire city was submerged. Sixty to seventy villages in the suburbs were completely flooded. The total estimated loss is no less than three million yuan. The largest flood record in Quanzhou city was June 1st, thirty-one years ago (Ji Si year). This flood was more than three feet higher, truly unprecedented in hundreds of years. From the morning of the 30th until 2:00 PM, the floodwaters entered the city, submerging eighty percent of the entire city. At 3:00 PM, the high tide reached the Quanzhou Yongchun Pharmacy entrance above the Kouzhang Alley entrance on the middle section of Zhongshan Road (South Street), from south to north. The water depth behind the South Gate Houshan was about thirteen feet. The Fumei and Customs Jubao Street areas were about nine feet deep. Yudiantou was fourteen feet high. The depth of water in Forts 5, 4, 3, 2, and 1 varied between thirteen and fourteen feet. Yiquan Garden Head was thirteen feet deep. The road from Yiquan Great Barrier Gate to Shuimen Alley entrance was about eight feet deep. The roads at Huaqiaoting, Pangongkou, and Zhuangfu Alley entrance were? eight to nine feet deep. North of Zhuangfu Alley entrance to Zhenfu Alley entrance, the ground was more sloped, and the depth varied, averaging about five feet. The water's tail reached Qiucuo Alley entrance near the top of the Shizi Street. West of Nanmalu, the low-lying areas of Xinmen Street were more than eight feet deep, Houcheng was five feet deep, Zhuangfu Alley was more than nine feet deep, Jinyu Alley was more than five feet deep, Maxia Alley was more than nine feet deep, the ditch was about thirteen feet deep, the entrance of Shuixian Temple was more than thirteen feet deep, Hua Alley was more than eight feet deep, Xiaohuangmen was more than nine feet deep, Xucuo Courtyard was eight feet, Xinluting and the ancient Rong Palace entrance were about nine feet. The section from Ximen Fengsheng to the city gate was thirteen feet deep, with the water surface almost level with the eaves. East of Nanmalu, the water depth in Tumen Street was seven feet. Daxixi Alley, Xiaoquanjian Alley, Chengtian Alley, Zhenfu Alley, Furen Alley, Yuxi Alley, etc., had varying depths of eight to nine feet to three to four feet. Other large and small alleys from Xinmen Street to West Street were also mostly flooded, with varying depths. Those on higher ground were spared. The villages such as Duansihu outside Ximen were completely submerged, with the water level equal to the rooftops, and the rooftops submerged daily. At the foot of the North Gate, the water was more than fourteen feet high. The nearby suburbs of Puming, Tian'an, Puren, Huayuantou, Tianbian, Tanwei, and Majiaopu were all flooded. From the 31st to the 1st, transportation was cut off. In the suburbs near Xinmen, the areas near the floating bridge and Huazhou in Dongmen, Dongbi, Caigongzhou, Pukou, and villages along the stream were a vast expanse. The villages of Jintoupou, Dahuan, Wuzhou, Houhuan, Hunei, and Dongwei outside Tumen were flooded to depths of five to six feet. Chenzhou, due to its low-lying location, had water reaching the rooftops.

On the 31st, the southeast wind had become gentle, with only intermittent showers. The sea tide also receded. After 4:00 PM, the water level began to drop. At 7:00 AM on the 1st, the water's tail receded to the Zhenfu Alley entrance on Zhongshan Road. After noon, all the roads on Zhongshan and the branch roads of Nanmen, except for the section from Huaqiaoting to Quanzhou Theater, where the water was inches deep, all revealed the road surface. It is estimated that transportation on the entire Zhongshan Road was restored after 10:00 AM. The floodwaters had completely receded overnight, but the alleys and ditches on the east side of Zhongshan Road were relatively low-lying and blocked, preventing water from draining. The alleys on the west side of Zhongshan South Road, being near the stream, would take one or two days to subside. In the suburbs, the areas outside Ximen and Beimen were still flooded, while Dongmen and Nanmen had receded. On the 2nd, Quanan cars only reached the Dongshan area, three miles outside Nanmen, from Anhai. From there, only small boats were relied upon for transportation to the city. The Fuzhou-Xiamen telegraph and telephone lines were cut off outside Quanzhou city. As of the 3rd, they had not been repaired. Currently, the Xiamen telegraph line only reaches Tong'an, and everything to the north is impassable.

On the 1st, all sectors of Quanzhou held an emergency meeting, attended by the Jinjiang County Government, the 9th Division Headquarters, the Jinjiang County Party Department, etc. County Magistrate Yu Gongwu presided over the meeting. It was decided to establish the Jinjiang All Circles Flood Relief Committee and to provide immediate relief by distributing steamed buns in the disaster areas for a provisional three days. It was also decided to set up shelters and use the county's original grain reserve savings of 5,000 yuan as collateral to borrow 3,000 yuan from the Bank of China for one month, with donations from all sectors to be used for repayment. On the other hand, a telegram was sent to the provincial government, requesting the Provincial Relief Committee to quickly handle emergency relief, as there are currently tens of thousands of displaced men and women in the disaster area, with thousands homeless.

According to Quanzhou news on the 3rd, the floodwaters in the city receded completely on the 1st. In the suburbs, the waters had not completely receded as of the 3rd, but the water was not very deep, and travel between the city and the countryside was possible. As of the 3rd, it was discovered that more than 700 houses had collapsed in the city, and more than 600 houses had collapsed in the suburban towns of Fuqiao and Xinmen, totaling more than 1,400 houses. As of the 3rd, the death toll was approximately 100. On the morning of the 31st, many corpses drifting from upstream were discovered in the Northwest Town in the suburbs.

The disaster in Nanan was more severe than in Jinjiang, and the affected area was even larger. The Honglai Wharf and the banks of the Zhiwei Stream, stretching over a hundred miles, were completely flooded. In Honglai Meirong village alone, 104 houses collapsed, and the water level was four to five feet higher than in the Ji Si year of thirty-one years ago. These hundred miles of farmland and villages were completely submerged. In the Yunwei area, the water had completely receded on the 31st, but the villages along the stream at the wharf were still a vast expanse. The water depth in the villages of Jintoupou, Dahuai, Wuzhou, Houhuan, Hunei, and Dongwei outside Tumen varied from five to six feet. In Chenzhou, due to its low-lying location, the water had already reached the rooftops.

On the 31st, the southeast wind had eased, with only intermittent showers. The sea tide had also receded. By 4:00 PM, the water level had started to drop. At 7:00 AM on the 1st, the water's tail had receded to the Zhenfu Alley entrance on Zhongshan Road. After noon, all the roads on Zhongshan and the branch roads of Nanmen, except for the section from Huaqiaoting to Quanzhou Theater, where the water was inches deep, had road surfaces visible. It is estimated that transportation on the entire Zhongshan Road was restored after 10:00 AM. The floodwaters had completely receded overnight, but the alleys and ditches on the east side of Zhongshan Road were relatively low-lying and blocked, preventing water from draining. The alleys on the west side of Zhongshan South Road, being near the stream, would take one or two days to subside. In the suburbs, the areas outside Ximen and Beimen were still flooded, while Dongmen and Nanmen had receded. On the 2nd, Quanan vehicles only travelled from Anhai to the Dongshan area, three miles outside Nanmen. From there, only small boats were relied upon for transportation to the city. The Fuzhou-Xiamen telegraph and telephone lines were cut off outside Quanzhou city. As of the 3rd, they had not been repaired. Currently, the Xiamen telegraph line only reaches Tong'an, and everything to the north is impassable.

(August 4th)

Hebei Province: Rapid Rise in River Levels

The disaster in southern Hebei is even worse than last year. The situation on the Taihang Dyke turns from critical to stable.

Baoding Dispatch: This year, the Yellow River flood has affected the three provinces of Hebei, Shandong, and Henan. The disaster situation in the three counties of Changyuan, Puyang, and Dongming in southern Hebei is even worse than last year. The people have suffered from years of successive disasters, and the tragic situation has reached its extreme. The provincial government has repeatedly received reports of disaster conditions from various counties, all requesting relief funds. Provincial Chairman Shang Zhen telegraphed the Central Government, earnestly requesting that the Central Government consider the financial difficulties of the people of Hebei Province and provide special relief. He also sent the Director of the Department of Construction, Lü Xian, to Beijing and Shanghai to meet with Minister of Finance Kong Xiangxi and Central Government officials to state the serious disaster situation in the province and the emptiness of the provincial treasury. Lü has now returned to Baoding. It is said that the Central Government is currently making overall plans for disaster relief, and Hebei's disaster relief is also included in the plans. The province only hopes that the Central Government will have a plan soon, so that hundreds of thousands of disaster victims can have hope of surviving.

The Taihang Dyke, which is crucial to the lifeline of Hebei Province, was in an extremely critical situation due to the impact of the water. Recently, under the supervision of the Department of Construction, various counties along the dyke have made desperate efforts to protect it, and the situation has turned from critical to stable. It has been found that the Taihang Dyke is currently divided into three sections for protection. Each section is headed by a local leader who is stationed on the dyke to direct the dyke protection. There are a total of 2,200 strong men protecting the dyke, stationed in sections. The first section, from Heyang Village in the east to Zhuzhuang Village in the west, has 720 strong men. A mat shed is built every half mile, with ten strong men inside at all times, patrolling day and night. In case of emergency, the strong men from each group will go to the dyke in unison. If there are not enough, strong men from villages more than ten miles away from the dyke will be gathered to increase the number. All strong men protecting the dyke on weekdays are recruited from villages within ten miles of the dyke according to land taxes. The second section, from east of the dike to Sundong Village in the west, has 680 strong men. The third section, from east of the Sanyi Dyke to west of Chang Village, has 800 strong men. In the event of heavy rain or a sudden rise in water levels, gongs will be sounded immediately to gather the masses to desperately protect the dyke. Recently, 1,500 strong men from villages outside the Beida Dyke and north of the Taihang Dyke have been called to the dyke to both engage in rescue and repair work, so it is fortunate that a temporary solution has been found.

Since the Yellow River overflowed, Changyuan County has also been affected by continuous gales and torrential rains, resulting in massive flooding in various places along the riverbank. The Yanggeng Dam was flooded, and thirteen zhang in the middle of the stone dam were washed away, with a width and depth of four to five feet. The rear of the western slope face embankment was also washed away by four to five zhang. Due to the vastness of the water, there is no accurate statistics of the damaged and incomplete parts of the dyke body. Recently, the water level inside the dyke has dropped by three feet, and the villagers are guarding it day and night. However, the situation is still worrying due to the seepage and waterlogging in various places along the riverbank. In Puyang County, due to flash floods in the mountains upstream of the Yellow River, the river water rose sharply, and the north dyke collapsed in more than twenty places. More than 120 villages inside the dyke, with more than 4,000 hectares of land and more than 50,000 households, all saw their houses, utensils, and livestock swept into the river. Approximately 25,000 people have drowned. The young and strong who escaped are now sleeping on the dyke, crying for food. Recently, continuous heavy rains have caused uncontrolled flooding. Eighty villages south of the Jindike have also suffered a catastrophe. Green seedlings in the fields have all been submerged in the vast ocean. The last hope for the disaster victims has been cut off. The people cannot even find rotten floc or stale grain to eat. Since the Yellow River flooded, the water in Dongming County has flowed backwards, with the water level equal to the dyke, two feet higher than last year's water level. Residents of villages inside the dyke have been unable to escape and are trapped in the water. Furthermore, the north wind has made the water more turbulent, and the south bank of the dike is in imminent danger. The 15th, 18th, and 20th embankments of the third section of the county are all leaking water and being scoured with deep trenches, which is extremely dangerous. The water is turbulent, and the embankment slope is being eroded, and the dyke root is also being hollowed out, causing the river water to penetrate and the dyke body to collapse. The water has overflowed again, and efforts are underway to rescue the disaster victims from danger. The Daqing River's water level has also risen sharply recently. Zhang Zhishi, director of the Daqing River Conservancy Bureau, telegraphed the provincial government, reporting that continuous heavy rains are causing the water level to continue to rise, and he is ordering the boatmen in various sections to step up their protection efforts. The South Canal has become even more turbulent and dangerous due to recent surges and continuous rain. The first, second, and third sections of the canal have all reached a critical stage, with the water level only a foot away from the bank. Jiang Yankun, director of the canal's conservancy bureau, specially came to the province yesterday to report on the canal situation and request instructions on flood prevention matters. It is said that if the canal continues to rise, the embankments are in danger of collapsing. The Department of Construction has specially ordered the directors of the Daqing and South Canal conservancy bureaus to take proper protective measures and report the water situation at any time.

Due to sudden torrential rains in the upper reaches of the Yongding River, flash floods have occurred, and the water level has risen sharply by about seven Chinese feet, and the water color has turned yellow, and the flow is extremely turbulent. The water level has not dropped in recent days and is still at nine meters. Within the territory of the North Fourth Section, embankment erosion and hidden movements have been continuously discovered, resulting in a very dangerous situation.

Wang Dingkui, the manager of the Fuyang River in southern Hebei, telegraphed the Department of Construction today to report that the river's water level had risen sharply due to continuous heavy rains and flash floods in the upper reaches. The river water at Yanjian Village in Cixian County was full, and the water level was higher than the river dyke, causing it to overflow for two to three days. As a result, more than twenty villages along the river in Handan County, including Liuzhuang, Zhangzhuang, Gaozhuang, Gongzhuang, Zuoxi Village, Nanbao Village, Dabao Village, Zhongbao Village, Wangqiebao, Junshibao, Zhangshi, etc., were submerged. The bridges on the Fuyang River are low, the water is shallow, and navigation has also been suspended. (August 6th)

Songjiang

The department issues an electric order to protect the seawall

Several sections of the seawall in this county near Jinshanwei are in danger. County Magistrate Jin, along with Xu Mojia, head of the Construction Section, have repeatedly planned repairs and prepared a budget to be submitted to the province for approval. Recently, during the typhoon season, seawall work is very important. Shen Baixian, Director of the Provincial Construction Department, telegraphed the county magistrate yesterday, stating that the seawalls of the four counties of Baoshan, Taicang, Songjiang, and Changshu are very important. Before the last big storm, each county was instructed to rush to prepare for protection on file. During the flood season, typhoons often occur, and the situation is dangerous. It is urgently telegraphed to the county magistrate to quickly inspect the area, strengthen the protection of the seawalls in the county, and quickly appoint construction personnel to supervise the seawall patrolmen to be stationed in the dangerous sections. The patrol situation should be reported to the Jiangnan Water Conservancy Engineering Office by express mail or telegram on a daily basis, and the names of the construction personnel assigned to the seawall should be reported first. At the same time, necessary materials should be quickly collected and stored for emergency rescue, and the dyke wardens should be strictly ordered to quickly repair the leaks. He should also adhere to the Jiangnan Water Conservancy Engineering Office for thorough handling and not be negligent. On the same day, the Water Conservancy Engineering Office also ordered Deputy Engineer Wang Zuorui to come to Songjiang to investigate. After receiving the order, County Magistrate Jin has already ordered patrolman Yang Yongnian to handle the matter seriously.

The detective team catches bandits

Recently, robberies have occurred frequently in Punan. Yang Shijie, captain of the detective team of the County Public Security Bureau, led his detectives to investigate. At about 6:00 AM on the 8th, while passing through Zhangzegang, they caught sight of two men covered in mud, holding clothing packages, and looking flustered. They immediately ordered them to stop and subjected them to inspection. A pistol, more than ten bullets, and men's and women's clothing were found on one of the men, clearly not good people. They were immediately arrested and taken back to the bureau for interrogation and investigation.

Suzhou

Companions' trip to Suzhou leads to bloodshed

Chen Baolian, who lives at Xinmatou outside Dadongmen in Shanghai, came to Suzhou with her friend Gu Azhen and others to play the day before yesterday. After arriving in Suzhou, at about 9:00 PM, they took a car to the airplane field outside Panmen to cool off. At about 12:00 AM, Gu asked Chen for eleven yuan, but Chen refused, leading to a conflict. Gu then pulled out a small knife and stabbed Chen Baolian three times in the throat, chest, and shoulder. Chen immediately fainted and fell to the ground. Gu then robbed Chen of the money and abandoned Chen in a ditch before escaping. After a while, Chen regained consciousness slightly, and it was already dawn. She then reported to the Guoxiang Street police station, who sent her to the General Bureau and then to the hospital for treatment. Meanwhile, the search for the assailant continues. It is reported that Chen's injuries are very serious and may be life-threatening.

The Construction Bureau rectifies vehicle licenses

Since the transfer of licenses for bicycles and self-use rickshaws in this county to the Construction Bureau, Director Zhang Fulin has repeatedly planned rectifications. In the past six months, the number of vehicles registered for licenses has increased dramatically, and the appearance of the city has gradually become more orderly. It is now learned that Director Zhang, in view of the recent increase in the number of vehicles for private use by civilians, and the fact that there are still a small number of vehicles without licenses, has dispatched vehicle management personnel to continue the inspection, aiming to achieve the goal of one vehicle, one license.

Yangzhou

Two deaths by shooting at Wanlu Temple

Zhenchuan, the abbot of Wanyuan Temple (about a mile from the town) in Caowang City Township, Fourth District, Jiangdu, (about 30 years old), and Ma Youtu, who lived in the temple with his wife, were shot and killed by bandits on the 6th. Women's fur coats and foreign ornaments, and monks' ceremonial clothing worth about 300 yuan were robbed. Kuang, Ma's wife, went to Xian Town yesterday (7th) to report to Director Bao of the First Branch of the Public Security Bureau, who reported it to the Jiangdu District Attorney's Office. This morning (8th), Prosecutor Meng Zhou rushed to inspect the scene and ordered the body to be prepared for burial, pending investigation and arrest of the murderers. According to the case details, more than ten years ago, the monk had an affair with the wife of Kuang Xiaosanzi, a cook in a certain camp stationed in Xian. Kuang's livelihood was unsustainable, and he divorced his wife. Later, he loaned money to Ma Youtu, who was in the business of tying flowers, to marry Kuang's wife, and they lived together in the temple. She was nominally Ma's wife, but in reality, she was the monk's woman. A few days ago, Kuang Xiaosanzi suddenly came to the temple and asked the abbot for his wife, but the monk sternly replied that you could not afford to ask for her back. Kuang gave a cold smile and left. On the day of the incident, neither the monk nor Ma were at home. Suddenly, two bandits came and asked where Youtu was. Ma's wife replied that he was not at home. The bandits pulled out pistols, forced Ma's wife and two servants into a room, and locked them up. In the afternoon, Ma returned and was shot three times and killed. The body was hidden. The bandits remained in the temple, waiting for the monk to return late at night, when he was also shot five times and killed. They then proceeded to loot extensively. At that time, the number of bandits increased, and they roared away. Liu Zonghan, captain of the Public Security Detective Team, was instructed by the county magistrate to solve the case within a time limit. In addition to sending detective police to investigate, he has scheduled to go to the scene of the incident with Detective Hu Keyin early tomorrow morning (9th) to investigate the situation. It is also reported that Kuang Xiaosanzi is now working as a squad leader in a certain armed unit in Taixian.

Current situation of requisitioning labor and collecting soil to repair embankments

Tang Jianzhong, Director of the Second Section of Jiangdu, and Shu Guohua, Director of the Construction Bureau, went to Shaobo to supervise the repair of the east dyke of the canal. According to the report from the Director of the Section to the county government, the recent situation of the dyke is not yet critical. During the great flood of the 20th year of the Republic, the water level mark from Gaoyou to the pier was above two zhang, but it has not yet reached one zhang. However, the situation is different this year, with the Yellow River encroaching south, so it is necessary to take precautions. They have supervised the relevant township chiefs of the Fourth and Seventh Districts to start requisitioning labor and collecting soil tomorrow. The cost of tea and water per unit has been increased to four cents, and the compensation for green seedlings is four yuan per mu. Wang Zizun, a flood officer, has been dispatched to handle the transport of labor with the county office.

Xiaoshan

Two houses robbed in one night

The home of Li Baoshan, deputy township chief of Taohu Township, Fourth District, Xiaoshan County, was well-off, leading to it being coveted by bandits. At about 2:00 AM on the 6th, more than ten bandits suddenly rushed in, immediately bound Li Baoshan and his family members, and threatened them to keep silent. They went upstairs, overturned boxes and chests, and looted at will. It is estimated that gold and silver jewelry and clothing worth more than 200 yuan were robbed. The victim has reported the loss to the township office and requested the county government to investigate and arrest the perpetrators. On the same night, the home of Xu Yuanfang, a resident of Deshengdian, Ganlu Township, Sixth District, was also robbed by more than ten bandits speaking a mixed dialect, armed with wooden-cased guns, who fired shots to intimidate the residents before entering and looting extensively. It is estimated that clothing, jewelry, and silver dollars totaling more than 400 yuan were robbed. A list of losses has been drawn up and reported to the county for investigation.

Local News

Kong Xiangxi Arrives in Shanghai Yesterday Morning to Discuss: The Central Government Decides to Retain President Wang; the Matter of Reforming the Monetary System Is Still Under Research and Planning; Outside Rumors That Currency Inflation Will Be Implemented Are Simply Ignorant

Central News Agency reports: Acting President of the Executive Yuan and Minister of Finance Kong Xianxi, accompanied by Fu Rulin, Chairman of the Yangtze River Water Conservancy Commission, and Peng Xuepei, a member of the Central Committee, left Beijing by night train at 11:00 PM the night before yesterday and arrived at the North Station at 7:15 AM yesterday morning. He went directly to West Asias Road to rest. At noon, he went to the Central Bank to handle important official business and met with newspaper reporters to issue important statements, details of which are recorded below:

Arrival in Shanghai Yesterday

After arriving in Shanghai yesterday morning, Kong went directly to his private residence to rest. At about 9:00 AM, he met with Zheng Lai, Director of the Customs Administration, to listen to a report on customs affairs. Zhang Gongquan, Vice President of the Central Bank, accompanied by Li Shuming, Deputy Manager of the International Savings Society, visited Kong at 9:30 AM to request instructions on the International Savings Society issue. The meeting lasted for more than an hour before they left. Supervisor Yan Zhuang and Hangzhou Customs Superintendent Fan Guang visited successively at around 10:30 AM, spoke briefly, and then left. Kong then went to the Central Bank at 11:00 AM to handle important official business, and successively met with Italian angel Roya Gugno, Italian Air Force Colonel Scalongne, Shen Wei Li Shizeng, Song Ziwen, Standing Committee Member of the National Economic Commission and Chairman of the Bank of China, Song Ziliang, General Manager of the National Products Bank, Qian Xinzhi, Manager of the Four Banks Preparation Treasury, and Xu Xinliu, General Manager of Zhejiang Industrial Bank.

Statements Made

Yesterday noon, Acting President Kong met with reporters from various newspapers at the Central Bank to answer various questions regarding President Wang's resignation. According to Kong, he had not yet heard of President Wang's resignation. When he was in Beijing, he heard that President Wang's health was gradually improving and that he would be able to return to Beijing in 20 days. If the reported resignation is indeed true, the Central Government will sincerely try to retain him and will definitely not let him retire. He plans to inspect the Yangtze River flood after he has some free time from official duties. As for the rumors that he will go to Lushan to escape the summer heat, that is not accurate. He currently has no time to escape the summer heat. Regarding the issue of reforming the monetary system, it is still under research and planning. In the future, it is planned to first recoin copper coins and then mint five-cent and ten-cent nickel coins, and twenty-five-cent and fifty-cent silver coins. The outside world has therefore mistakenly rumored that the government will implement currency inflation, which is simply ignorant.

Cai Yuanpei Set to Depart for Qingdao This Morning; Ordered to Retain President Wang

Cai Yuanpei, a member of the Central Committee, is scheduled to take the China Merchants Bureau's Haiheng ship to Qingdao at 9:00 AM this morning to visit Executive Yuan President Wang Jingwei, who is recuperating in Qingdao. It is reported that Cai and Ye Chucang, Secretary-General of the Central Party Headquarters, are going to Qingdao one after the other, both with the order of the Central Government to sincerely persuade President Wang to stay.

Yesterday Morning's Hurricane Veered, Shanghai Spared from Storm, Maritime Traffic Resumes

According to the Astronomical Observatory's report yesterday, the Pacific hurricane, which was heading directly towards Shanghai the day before yesterday, had already reached Shanghai. However, at 6 PM that evening, the wind direction shifted northward, encountering Suzhou's western area, crossing the Yangtze River and reaching Nantong. Therefore, Shanghai was spared from disaster. By 6 AM yesterday morning, the Astronomical Observatory's records indicated that it had already left Nantong towards the Yellow Sea, located at 33 degrees north latitude and 122 degrees east longitude, with the wind direction northeast and the center at 60 nautical miles, blowing towards Korea. After learning that the hurricane's direction had shifted north and its center would not hit Shanghai, the Jianghai Customs immediately lifted the storm warning yesterday morning, removing the black ball from the customs clock tower flagpole. As a result, the ships that had been delayed by the storm the previous day, including Ningbo's Sanbei's "Ningxing," China Merchants' "Xinjiangtian," Yangtze River's China Merchants' "Jianghua," Taikoo's "Datong," Jardine Matheson's "Xin Pinghe," Nanhua's Taikoo's "Yuezhou," Fuzhou's Sanbei's "Wanxiang," and Wenzhou-Taizhou's Lianan's "Chuanshan," all resumed normal sailing yesterday morning. The Taikoo's Hong Kong-bound "Niuzhuang" and China Merchants' Beiyang-bound "Xinfeng," which had failed to arrive the previous day, also arrived yesterday morning. The China Merchants Bureau's "Haiheng" ship arrived in Shanghai yesterday. According to its crew, it encountered a hurricane and heavy rain outside Shantou Port and stopped sailing to avoid the storm for as long as 48 hours. Many other ships also stopped to avoid the storm at the same time, fortunately without any accidents. Also, the bureau's "Yushun" ship encountered a hurricane in the MS oupurnoud sea area and dropped anchor to stop sailing to avoid danger. The Wenzhou-bound "Neihaiyan" ship also received a hurricane warning in of Guarantin and immediately stopped sailing to avoid being hit. Furthermore, the "Gongping" ship sailing to Lotsin Boy and the "Xinming" ship sailing to 120 degrees 30 minutes east longitude and 30 degrees 30 minutes north latitude all received hurricane warnings and stopped sailing together. They all sent telegrams to Shanghai yesterday, saying that they would resume sailing after the storm passed.

Huachang Steamship Report: Safely Arrived in Keelung Last Night

Sheltering from the storm in Xiamen on the morning of the 3rd.

Huasheng Steamship Co., Ltd. sent a letter to this newspaper yesterday stating that the "Huachang Steamship Has Not Sent Telegrams for Seven Days" was published in the local news section of your newspaper. This morning (the 9th), our company received a telegram sent from Keelung, as well as letters from the chief mate and chief engineer of the Huachang ship. According to them, they set sail from Hongji on July 29, passed through Hong Kong on the afternoon of the 1st, and suddenly received a weather report by wireless, knowing that a hurricane was approaching. Therefore, they arrived outside Xiamen Port on the morning of the 3rd to shelter from the storm. They safely arrived in Keelung last night, taking on coal and will be able to set sail. This is hereby communicated.

Rickshaws in Nanshi and the French Concession Resumed Work Yesterday

The Municipal Government and the Taxpayers' Association Agreed on Two Principles: Registration Fees Waived and Registration Time Extended — No Towing into the French Concession Until Officially Resolved —

Regarding the strike of rickshaw pullers in the French Concession, the Party and government authorities believed that it was related to traffic order, so they instructed the rickshaw guild to relay the message to the rickshaw owners, who then consulted all the rickshaw pullers to resume work first and wait for the government to handle it. At 6 AM yesterday morning, the rickshaw pullers resumed work, and the order was very good. However, it was limited to Nanshi because the licenses of the French Concession had been removed.

Temporary Scheduled Traffic Range

The rickshaw traffic range is specified as (A) in the Shanghai South area: (1) Zhonghua Road from Laoximen to Xiaodongmen, inside and outside the city walls; (2) Only the Huajie (Chinese area) sections of Minguo Road from Laoximen to Xiaodongmen, including Fangbang Road, Xiaobeimen, Xinqiao Street, Laobeimen, Xinbeimen, Xinkaihe, and Xinxiaodongmen. However, they cannot cross the iron gates of the French Concession; (3) Heping Road, Zhaozhou Road, and Xieqiao cannot cross the iron gates; (B) in the Shanghai West area: (1) Xujiahui along the Huajie Xiexu South Road, Jinji Bridge, Fenglin Bridge, and Fahua Town, but not across the bridges.

Fill out Registration Forms to Retrieve Detained Vehicles

The vehicles detained by the French Concession police stations can only be returned after the rickshaw pullers register. At 9 PM the night before, the guild sent standing committee members Qiu Chunshan and Zhang Huaiyang, together with Cheng Zhusun and Shang Mujing, members of the Taxpayers' Association and the Municipal Federation, to visit Du Yuesheng, the Chinese director of the French Concession, to report on the progress, fill out registration forms for each vehicle and each person according to the regulations, and retrieve the detained vehicles for business.

Extended Period for Preparation

The result of the consultation between the rickshaw merchant representatives at Du's residence, in addition to registering the rickshaw pullers and retrieving the detained vehicles, was to apply for registration for all the more than 6,000 rickshaws that had not been detained, according to the regulations of the French Concession. If the registration fee can be reduced after Du negotiates with the French authorities, the police station will refund it. The period is extended to the end of the year to allow the rickshaw pullers to prepare fully.

Issue Additional Licenses to Restore Traffic

On the evening of the 8th, the guild ordered the rickshaw owners to hand in their French Concession licenses to the guild. Yesterday, the rickshaw merchants consulted at the Penglai Teahouse and decided to return the French Concession notices. The French Concession rickshaws resumed traffic at 9 AM, but most of the rickshaw pullers were unwilling to pull in the French Concession, so the number was not as crowded on the road as it was before August 6.

The Social Affairs Bureau Sent Personnel to Supervise the Resumption of Work

Because the Social Affairs Bureau was afraid that the rickshaw owners and rickshaw pullers would still have strong prejudices, at 9 AM yesterday morning, it sent Wang Gang, the director of the Huigong Division, and Zhu Zhulin, a mediator, to earnestly advise the rickshaw owners and rickshaw pullers to maintain traffic as the top priority. At the same time, they also supervised the resumption of work by the rickshaw pullers and went to various roads to inspect the situation, saw that the order was good, and immediately returned to the bureau to report.

The Authorities Agreed on Two Principles

The municipal government attached great importance to this case. Yesterday afternoon, it specially sent Secretary Geng Jiaji, Wang Gang, the director of the Huigong Division of the Social Affairs Bureau, Du Ri and Shang Mujing of the French Concession Taxpayers' Chinese Association, and Qiu Chunshan and Zhang Huaiyang, representatives of the guild, to negotiate together and agree on two principles: (1) Rickshaw puller registration is free of charge; (2) The registration time is extended by two months, which will be negotiated by the municipal government and the Taxpayers' Association with the French authorities.

Prevent Leaks to Avoid Losses

The Special District Office of the Rickshaw Industry Guild of this city convened an emergency meeting of directors at 10 AM yesterday morning. More than ten people, including Gu Songmao, Hou Shaoan, and Jin Chunlin, attended the meeting as scheduled. After Chairman Gu Songmao reported the purpose of the meeting, the elbow discussion items were: (1) The case of the leakage trend in the Public Concession vehicles driving into the French Concession. It was resolved to notify the rickshaw merchants to inform the rickshaw pullers to temporarily stop driving into the French Concession to avoid losses; (2) The case of the French Concession rickshaw pullers opposing registration and requesting assistance. It was resolved to provide assistance according to law; (3) The case of the insufficient number of registered rickshaw pullers in the Public Concession. It was resolved to send a letter to the authorities requesting continuous registration. Finally, the chairman reported that the case of the representative suing Zheng Fazhu for compensation for losses had been scheduled for sentencing on the morning of the 13th of this month. The meeting was adjourned. As for the conflict between the Yuebu and the rickshaw pullers on the 6th of this month, in order to facilitate negotiations, the rickshaw owners and rickshaw pullers specially designated responsible representatives to handle all matters, including rickshaw merchants Qiu Chunshan, Zhang Huaiyang, Yu Dakin, and rickshaw pullers Xu Hongsheng, Zhou Yongcai, Yang Yougui, and Li Asi, a total of seven people, as fully authorized representatives to resolve all unresolved cases together with the Party and government authorities.

Notify Rickshaw Merchants to Avoid Accidents

The Special District Office notified the rickshaw merchants yesterday, "Because the French Concession authorities forced rickshaw pullers to register this time, it caused a major trend on the 6th of this month, which eventually led to a strike by rickshaw pullers in various parts of Shanghai South. Our special district rickshaw merchants have been subjected to leakage and sabotage, and the losses are incalculable. If we do not take precautions, how can we imagine it? We must say that our special district colleagues should entrust the rickshaw pullers to never drive in without authorization until the municipal government is responsible for handling the unresolved matters to avoid accidents. In addition to sending a special letter of notification, we will publish a notice in Shen Xin and other newspapers. Regarding the registration of rickshaw pullers in the British Concession, we hope that the rickshaw owners will inform the rickshaw pullers to drag them to the registration office before the 15th of this month, and do not make mistakes," and so on.

After the expiration of the period, there will be a limited common period of six months (ie, from January 1, 25th year to June 30th). After the expiration date, it will be invalid." Ministry of Industry and Commerce Seeks to Relieve Industry and Commerce Formulated Three Measures

Researching Control to Increase International Trade Formulating Protection Policies to Investigate Exports

According to Xinxin News Agency, the Ministry of Industry and Commerce, in view of the recent bankruptcy of the rural economy in our country, the huge trade deficit in international trade, and the resulting economic poverty of the people, and the extreme depression of industry and commerce, has now formulated three relief measures and is actively proceeding with them. They are recorded below:

Increase Exports

(1) In recent years, international economic policies have often changed. Either low currencies, managed foreign exchange, controlled trade with quota systems, and increased tariffs, etc., all possible ways to increase exports and prohibit imports are implemented as much as possible. The commodities exported from our country, such as silk, tea, silk, cotton, and egg products, are all affected by increased taxes and quota pressure in various countries, resulting in a decreasing number of exported goods. We are also studying control measures, and once they are drafted, we will consult with relevant departments to discuss effective remedial measures to make fundamental relief. At the same time, it will be held in the middle of this month.

Protection Policies

(2) The business situation of our country's exported commodities is rarely investigated in detail, and accurate statistics, and the export situation, are not known. We are currently drafting a form to order local governments in various provinces and cities to investigate the business situation of various exported commodities to serve as a reference for formulating protection policies. We will also investigate the nature of the products, and if they can be sold overseas, we will guide the merchants to find ways to promote and try to sell them, and order the consulates abroad to introduce them on their behalf. At the same time, we will collect samples and forward them to domestic manufacturers for imitation to promote sales.

Investigate Exports

To promote foreign trade as much as possible, it is necessary to understand foreign commercial information. Therefore, European and American countries often send foreign commercial investigation missions. The overseas Chinese in our country are scattered abroad, and they have suffered extremely heavy losses in the recent global depression. If we want to seek considerable relief, we must have accurate investigations. Minister Chen, in view of this, personally went to Nanyang last year to inspect various properties. In addition to actively preparing for the investigation team to go to various factories in Siam to investigate the commercial situation, we will continue to send personnel to Europe, the United States, and Japan to conduct similar investigations to make improvements. All the candidates and budget for the inspection team to Siam are being reviewed and will soon be seen in fact.

Zhejiang Province Plans to Issue Six Million Yuan in Treasury Bonds Once Visited Finance Minister Kong in Beijing to Inquire About Everything

Twenty-Three Approved for Establishment in Recent Months All Unregistered Ones Will Be Banned

According to Xinxin News Agency, in order to prevent newly established banks in various places from opening business without completing registration procedures, and once they go bankrupt, affecting depositors and social finance, the Ministry of Finance strictly enforces supervision and registration. The Ministry recently listed 23 banks that were approved for registration from October last year to the end of June this year and sent them to the provincial governments and the Shanghai Municipal Government for verification. If there are any banks or money houses that have been established without approval, please transfer them to the ban to comply with the law. The consultation and approved banks are recorded as follows:

Consultation with Various Provinces and Cities Original Text

Regarding the name, organization, paid-up capital, location of the head office, and the date of approval of registration of approved banks, and the issuance of business licenses and numbers, etc., this Ministry has compiled a list and sent it to your provincial and municipal governments for verification. If you encounter any unapproved and unregistered banks or money houses, please order them to quickly follow the regulations, prepare various registration documents, and submit them to the Ministry for verification. At the same time, pay attention to supervision at any time. If the approved banks establish branches in various provinces and cities, they should send the registration approved by the Ministry and the establishment of branches to the local government for verification and record. If there are any branches that have been established without approval, the local government should transfer them to the Ministry for verification in order to comply with the law and facilitate investigation. Now, from October of the 23rd year to the end of June of this year, there are many more banks that have been approved for registration and reissued business licenses by this Ministry.
