Guangdong Fellow Countrymen Association Requests Guangdong Province to Abolish the Control of Local Sugar

The Guangdong Provincial Industry Management Office's control of local sugar has aroused great resentment among the people of fifteen prefectures in Chaozhou and Meizhou. Local sugar is one of the agricultural products, and farmers work hard all year round, relying on it for food and clothing. At a time when the countryside is declining, if registration and suspension of transportation are implemented, it will be like draining the pond to catch the fish. The lives of millions of creatures will inevitably perish together. Now, local sugar is piled up like mountains and cannot be transported for sale. At this time of scorching summer heat, there is even a risk of dissolution. The Guangdong Fellow Countrymen Association in Shanghai specially requested the situation from Chen Jitang, Commander-in-Chief of the First Group Army, Lin Yunge, Chairman of the Province, Qu Mangpu, Director of the Department of Finance, and He Qiqin, Director of the Department of Construction, and requested that the order be withdrawn immediately to maintain production and alleviate the suffering of the people. Every word is a tear, and I cannot bear to read it. This is also something that those who care about the people's suffering should pay special attention to. The original submission is recorded as follows:

Through Traffic on the Shanghai-Guangdong Highway: The Entire Route is 1,779 Miles Long, Reachable by Car in 122 Hours

The Shanghai-Guangdong Highway has now been completed under the supervision of the National Economic Council's Highway Department and the Guangdong Provincial Highway Engineering Bureau. A private car has already traversed the entire route once, with excellent results. However, both authorities reportedly do not intend to hold a traffic opening ceremony. Our East China News Agency reporter has investigated and reports the details as follows:

Places Passed

The Shanghai-Guangdong Highway follows the Shanghai-Hangzhou Highway to Hangzhou, then from Hangzhou to Yushan, Nanchang, Changsha, Hengshan, Ganzhou, Dayu, Nanxiong to Shaoguan, then turns to Shantou and arrives at Guangzhou. The entire road surface engineering, from Shanghai to Shaoguan, was supervised by the National Economic Council's Highway Department, while the section from Shaoguan to Guangzhou was supervised by the Guangdong Provincial Highway Engineering Bureau.

Segmented Completion

The Shanghai-Guangdong Highway is 1,779 miles long. The section from Shanghai to Shaoguan is 1,023 miles, and the Highway Department of the National Economic Council was responsible for supervising the construction in the various provinces and cities it passed through. Since the council began supervising the construction in May of the 21st year [of the Republic, i.e., 1932], the section between Shanghai and Hangzhou (i.e., the Shanghai-Hangzhou Highway) was completed and opened to traffic earlier in the previous year. The sections from Hangzhou to Yushan, Nanchang, Changsha, Hengshan, Ganzhou, Dayu, Nanxiong, and Shaoguan have also been actively expedited by the Zhejiang, Jiangxi, and Hunan provinces, and were fully completed last month. Branch lines between the provinces have been opened to traffic one after another. The section from Shaoguan to Guangzhou is 756 *li* long and was supervised by Guangdong Province. Since the province urged the Highway Engineering Bureau to start construction in the autumn of the 22nd year [of the Republic, i.e., 1933], it has been two years, and it was also completed last month. Therefore, the entire Shanghai-Guangdong line can now be directly traversed by car. Because the authorities of each province along the way held a traffic opening ceremony after each section of the province was completed (as with the Shanghai-Hangzhou Highway), both sides plan not to hold another traffic opening ceremony.

First Through Traffic

After the road was completed, Mr. Ni Tuosheng from Fujian, along with two friends, drove his own Model Y Ford car on a full-line test drive on the 21st of last month to investigate the actual situation of highway development along the way. According to Mr. Ni upon his return to Shanghai, this trip followed the above-mentioned route, going directly from Shanghai to Guangzhou. The travel time was calculated as 57 hours for the Shanghai to Shaoguan section and 65 hours for the Shaoguan via Shantou to Guangzhou section, for a total of 122 hours to reach Guangzhou directly. The latter section is shorter in mileage, but took more time because the road between Shantou and Guangzhou is rugged and difficult to travel, and also requires detours. The results of this trip were excellent. The highways in Hunan Province are based on science everywhere, neat, solid, and the best in the provinces, not much inferior to those in Europe and America. Although our country has been working hard to build highways in recent years, there are not many people who drive for long distances. Mr. Ni's perseverance is admirable. It is also heard that the gasoline used this time was only 106 gallons.

American and Japanese Shipping Companies Establish Price Reduction Agreement for Hong Kong and Shanghai

Implementing Competitive Shipping This Month

The Pacific shipping lines are mostly owned by the United States and Japan. Now, due to competition in business, a price reduction agreement has been established between Hong Kong and Shanghai. Passenger and freight rates have been reduced across the board. It has already been implemented from this month. First class has been reduced to 45 yuan for a single trip and 81 yuan for a round trip. Second class has been reduced to 30 yuan for a single trip and 54 yuan for a round trip, and two types of 25 yuan and 45 yuan. Third class is divided into two types of 10 yuan and 15 yuan. All are calculated in US dollars. It is heard that those who have joined this agreement include Nippon Yusen Kaisha, Dollar Steamship Lines, Federal Steam Navigation Company, United States Lines, and Canadian Pacific Steamship Company, etc.

The 13th Lottery Drawing Was Held Yesterday

The First Prize is Number 233781, Sold by the Dayun Company's Retail Department. The Next Drawing is Scheduled for September 6th

Since the National Government's Aviation Highway Construction Lottery changed its method starting from the 13th period, there are more opportunities to win, so sales have been very strong. At 2:00 PM yesterday, the 13th lottery drawing was held as usual at Yiyuan Park in public, and there were many spectators. After Committee Member Wang Xiaolai and Director Chen Hong reported on the revised method, the drawing began. The first prize was number 233781, which was drawn at about 2:45 PM. It was found that it was sold in strips by the retail department of Dayun Company. The winner is unknown. The 14th lottery tickets will be issued immediately, and the drawing will be held at the original location on September 6th. The details of yesterday's drawing are recorded as follows:

Increased Number of Prizes Compared to Previous Issues

The Aviation Lottery has been issued up to the 13th period. The office previously obtained the approval of the Ministry of Finance to change the method, which has been implemented from this period. There are a total of 300,000 lottery numbers, and each number is still sold for ten yuan and sold in strips. Although the first prize has been reduced to 250,000 yuan, the other smaller prizes are more than before, and ten additional prizes are added for the upper and lower associated numbers of the first and second prizes. However, in order to simplify the drawing procedures, the original fifth and sixth prizes all use the last three characters for matching numbers, so although there are many winning numbers, the drawing is very fast and convenient.

Representatives from All Parties Supervise

At 2:00 PM yesterday, the 13th lottery tickets were held at Yiyuan Park on Albert Road. Those present for supervision included Yu Hongqi from the Control Yuan, Luo Panhui from the Municipal Government, Chen Zheqing from the Municipal Chamber of Commerce, Lin Kanghou from the Municipal Banking Association, Zhang Shou from the Ministry of Finance, Sun Wenjia from the National Aviation Construction Association, Li Ping from the Second Special District Local Court, banker Wu Yunzhai, Hu Zutong, Dayun Company’s Yu Yanfang, lottery office committee member Wang Xiaolai, Xu Xinliu, director Chen Hong, etc., and about a thousand Chinese and foreign guests. In order to make the guests understand the drawing procedures, the office specially sent receptionists to lead the guests to inspect the drawing balls and prize balls before the drawing.

Inspect Drawing Balls

After the number balls, prize level balls, etc. were inspected by the supervisors and guests, Committee Member Wang Xiaolai reported, saying, "The lottery tickets for this period are being drawn here, and we welcome everyone to come and supervise. The method of this period has been slightly changed and has been publicly announced in the newspaper. Our office strives for perfection in the method, and its drawing procedures have also been improved several times, becoming more and more perfect, so that guests can see it clearly at a glance. Now that the drawing balls, etc. have been inspected, the drawing will begin." Then, Director Chen translated it in English, shook the copper machine balls evenly, and started the drawing.

Number Ball Drawing Procedures

The copper machine balls for the drawing are still three in number. The A machine ball is larger, storing 3,000 number balls. The B machine ball stores 100 number balls. The C machine ball stores 125 wooden balls for prize levels, divided into first, second, third, and fourth prizes. Each ball is connected to a glass container with a copper groove. After each winning number is drawn, the staff broadcasts it throughout the venue with a loudspeaker and displays it on a blackboard. All major prizes are delivered by the executor to the supervisors for verification and photographed to show solemnity.

Situation of Drawing Various Prizes

The drawing started at 2:00 PM, and at about 2:45, the first prize was drawn, which was number 233781. It was found that it was sold in strips by the retail department of Dayun Company. The winner has not yet been identified. There were also two second prizes, ten third prizes, and thirty-two fourth prizes, which were also distributed through the company. The first to fourth prizes were drawn at about 4:00 PM, and then the fifth and sixth prizes were drawn. First, the 1,000 wooden balls were sealed, and after being inspected by the supervisors, they were poured into the C machine ball and shaken evenly. The first draw was "993" for the fifth prize. All those with the same last three characters won the prize. The second and third draws were "184" and "795" for the sixth prize. All those with the same last three characters won the prize. All prizes were drawn at 4:30 PM before the event dispersed.

Numbers for Each Major Prize Level

The numbers for each prize level are as follows: First prize "233781", additional prize for associated numbers of the first prize "233780", "233782", second prize "149657", "175013", "181938", "253223", additional prize for associated numbers of the second prize "149656", "149658", "175012", "175014", "181937", "181939", "253222", "253224", seventh prize last two characters "81", eighth prize last one character "1", remaining prizes omitted.

Scheduled Start of Prize Redemption

The prize money for this period will be paid in seven days. The office posted a notice saying, "It has been found that the 13th National Government Aviation Highway Construction Lottery was drawn in public at Yiyuan Park this month. The prize money for the winning lottery tickets in this period has been entrusted by this office to the Central Bank, Bank of China, and Bank of Communications in various places for payment. The valid period for prize redemption is from August 17th of this year to January 30th of the 25th year [of the Republic, i.e., 1936]. Overdue will be invalid. This is hereby announced. Director Chen Hong. It is heard that the 14th lottery tickets are scheduled to be drawn at the original location on September 6th, and the lottery tickets will be issued from today.

Rickshaw Pullers Mutual Aid Society Was Sabotaged Yesterday

Distributing Fake Leaflets. The Society Explains the Situation

Yesterday, leaflets signed "Shanghai Rickshaw Pullers Mutual Aid Society Declaration" and "Shanghai Rickshaw Pullers Mutual Aid Society Promotion, Relief Undertakings, Giving 20,000 of Rice, Giving 40,000 of Clothes, Lending 400,000, Fellow Members, Now the Market in Shanghai, Is Really Bad to the Extreme, You Must Also Be Suffering Greatly, Moreover, Now Is the Time of Scarcity, Although You Run Under the Hot Sun Every Day, But the Income is Very Little, Even Can Not Support the Whole Family, I am Afraid That Even My Own Life, Maybe, Can Not Be Maintained, We Understand This Most Painful and Difficult Life Very Well, Now to Relieve Your Pain Has Been Done, 20,000 of Rice, 40,000 of Clothes, Waiting for You All to Receive, and We Have Recruited Enough Rickshaw Pullers Savings Bank Capital 500,000 Especially Set Up Loan Department, If You Have Any Expenses, You Can Come to the Bank of This Association to Borrow, But Each Member Is Limited to at Most Ten Dollars, All the Above, You Can Go to the General Association on Jiaxing Road, Ask Director-General Zhang Dengyun, Request to Issue It, I Think You Got This Good News, Must Be Very Happy, and You Must Support the Work of This Association and the Competence of the Director-General, etc.," were distributed on the roads within the concession and in Zhabei and the Southern City, intending to instigate the general public and rickshaw pullers in the concession to go to the Rickshaw Pullers Mutual Aid Society to make trouble. Yesterday, the responsible person of the Mutual Aid Society issued the following statement:

"Our Association is dedicated to providing welfare undertakings for rickshaw pullers within the concession, improving all aspects of their lives and treatment. Five offices have been established, and there are more than twenty types of practical welfare work (see the newspapers of August 5th). However, where there is profit, competition is bound to be fierce, so there are often people who do various things to sabotage the economy of this association. There are many reasons for this kind of sabotage. Because they cannot participate in the Mutual Aid Association and control everything, they express jealousy and resentment, which is not worth the recognition of those who know better. Yesterday at 1:30 PM, many people holding the following leaflets came to the General Association and the Southern City Branch, demanding that the items listed on the leaflets be issued. The staff of this association persuaded them not to be manipulated by others, repeatedly enlightened them, and dispersed them after persuading them in a good manner, without causing any trouble. From 1:30 PM to 4:00 PM, the number of rickshaw pullers who came to the association to ask for items reached six or seven hundred. Among them, a rickshaw puller named Zhang Wanhe, registration number 5381, pointed out on the spot that this kind of leaflet was given by Zhu Fengxiang, in a number of seven or eight sheets, and Zhu Fengxiang instructed him to distribute them to each rickshaw puller. At that time, the Jiaxing Road Police Station and the bailiff also arrived. After inquiring about the details of this association, they took Zhang Wanhe away for questioning. After 4:00 PM, a rickshaw puller led a person who was distributing leaflets on the road to the association. This association handed him over to the police for handling. According to the confession, they were also instigated by Zhu Fengxiang et al. on Liyuan Road in the Southern City to distribute them, and they promised them a major reward in the future. At the same time, it happened to be the time when the Board of Directors of this Association was holding a standing meeting, and Zhu Fengxiang, Xu Zhulin, Cang Gongwen, etc. came to the association and declared that they would announce the accounts of this association, demand that the items listed on the leaflets be issued, and must meet with the directors. They were also taken to the police station by the bailiff for handling. Although there was a slight conflict among the dozens of people who came with them, it was quickly suppressed by the detectives and pacified."

Zheng Yu Gui's Wife Commits Suicide by Poison; Her Family Accuses Him of Assault

Yesterday, the medical certificate of injury was certified by the doctor; the court still needs to investigate and postpone the hearing.

Zheng Yu Gui, a Chaozhou native and the small proprietor of the Yongning Pawnshop at 22 Chengdu Road, and his wife, Chen Lianna, committed suicide by opium smoking on the 19th of last month. Because she left a suicide note stating that all her jewelry was in the bathroom on the third floor of her mother's home at 84 Yugu Village, Yugu Road, Zheng negotiated with his mother-in-law, Chen Yang. The latter also reported to the Chengdu Road police station that her son-in-law had beaten her daughter on March 12th of last year, causing injuries. After investigation by detective Huang Fu Sen, Zheng filed a public lawsuit, which was summoned once by the Special Court. The details of the bribes have been recorded in this newspaper on the 3rd of this month. Yesterday morning, Judge Ye Sheng Chao summoned them in the Second Criminal Court. According to Zhang Shi Zhu, the lawyer of the police station, Dr. Dao from Renji Hospital, who was ordered by the court to summon, had arrived in court. Dao then submitted the case, proving that the injury certificate of the deceased was signed by him, but he did not know who caused the injury. The court then asked Chen Yang if there was any other evidence besides the maid, Lu Wu. She replied that there was no other proof. When questioned, Zheng Yu Gui stated that the relationship between him and his wife was quite harmonious. Chen Lianna's suicide was due to the fact that his family was old-fashioned, and she felt that she could not freely go out to play. Zheng's defense lawyer, Chen Ting Rui, immediately stood up and stated one point, asking the court to pay attention, saying that the opium Chen Lianna took when she committed suicide came from her mother's home. The court, needing further investigation, ordered a postponement of the hearing.

Robbers Gun Down Shop Owner on Dongchang Road, Pudong

The Public Security Bureau is close by, yet the robbers are rampant to this extent.

Hu De Sheng, a native of Changzhou, opened a small cigarette paper shop (said to have less than 100 yuan in capital) at No. 71 Tian, Bingchang Road, Dongchang Road, Lan Ni Du, Pudong. At about 9 o'clock the night before, three robbers suddenly broke into the shop, threatened with guns, and searched everywhere, but found nothing of value. The robbers were very disappointed. Because the drawer of the account case was tightly locked, the robbers forced the shop owner to ask where the key was. Knowing that it was difficult to escape, Hu De Sheng said that the key was upstairs and allowed him to go and get it. After he finished speaking, he turned around and went upstairs. At that time, only Hu's wife, Hu Wu, was in the shop. Seeing that the robbers were fierce, she shouted for help. The robbers were angry at her publicity and immediately opened fire, hitting the left temple of the woman. The bullet did not penetrate, and the woman fell to the ground, bleeding profusely. Seeing that they had caused trouble, the robbers had no time to rob and fled in a swarm. Hu De Sheng, who was upstairs, suddenly heard a gunshot and knew something was wrong. He rushed downstairs and saw his wife lying in a pool of blood, already dead. He couldn't help but grieve loudly over the body. When the police on duty heard the news and rushed over, the robbers had already disappeared without a trace. They immediately reported to the Pudong Branch. Yesterday morning, they instructed the local Bao Lu Shun Long to report to the local court for an autopsy. Prosecutor Zhang Zi was then commissioned to lead examiner Shen Qi Xiu to Pudong for an autopsy. They instructed the corpse handler to put the body in a coffin and wait for the arrest of the murderer. The location of the incident is very close to the Pudong Branch. The robbers dared to be so rampant, truly showing a lack of fear of the law.

Stock Broker from Jin Yu Securities Embezzles Huge Amount of Securities

Worth over 33,000 yuan; when the situation became urgent, he surrendered himself—two accomplices are at large and have not been caught.

Wei Ting Rong's eldest son, Yuan Sheng, a well-known figure in this city who once served as the commander of the French Concession Volunteer Corps, has recently been repeatedly losing money due to operating public bonds and securities with Gan Deng Lai, a runner from Jin Yu Securities. Gan could not stand it and absconded with a large sum of money from the company. He was arrested a few days ago, while Wei Yuan Sheng also fled without a trace because he was suspected of being an important suspect and the court issued a warrant for his arrest. Now, because the main suspect is at large, the case may not be easily concluded for a while, so we will describe its process and the feelings of the public as follows:

Jin Yu Securities

The company is located at 16 Qingyuan Lane, Beiyuan Road, between the British and French concessions. It was founded by Shen Chang Geng, and the current manager is Gan Yun Qiao, a native of Yuyao. Gan Deng Lai is also from the same hometown. Gan Deng Lai serves as the company's runner, recommended by Gan Ting Hui, specializing in soliciting transactions and delivering certificates. Wei Ting Rong's son, Wei Yuan Sheng, has often bought and sold securities in the name of Wei Yuan Sheng in recent years, and gradually became acquainted with Gan Deng Lai. Over time, their friendship became deep. Recently, they jointly operated, but both failed, losing more than 16,000 yuan.

Gan Lai

lacked financial resources, and thus conceived the idea of embezzlement, hoping to make up for it. On the morning of July 29, Jin Yu transferred 60,000 yuan of 22-year customs treasury bills and interest coupons due in July of this year to Gan Deng Lai for encashment at the Bank of China and the Central Bank, equivalent to 33,053.56 yuan. He took the opportunity to steal it and flee. Gan Yun Qiao, the manager of Jin Yu, waited until the day before yesterday and still did not see him return. He entered his empty bedroom to check, and found that his clothes and other items were gone. He then knew that Gan Deng Lai

had been planning for a long time

and immediately reported to the police station, offering a reward for his arrest. It turned out that Gan Deng Lai took the interest money from the bank that day and, together with the coupons, took refuge in Wei Yuan Sheng's home at 194 Xujiahui Road in the French Concession. By the evening of August 1, Gan Lai felt that the outside world was very tense and that he could not avoid the matter by hiding, so he surrendered to the police station with coupons worth 5,000 yuan. The next morning, he was sent to the First Special District Court for questioning. Because the stolen goods were not complete,

Wei Yuan Sheng was greatly involved.

In addition to detaining the defendant, a warrant was issued to search for Wei Yuan Sheng. That afternoon, the police station sent detectives Su Chang Sheng and Li Yi to the French Concession Police Station and dispatched more detectives to Wei Yuan Sheng's home to arrest him, but they did not find Wei's trace. They only found some hidden coupons. They then went to Yuan Sheng's residence, 999 next door, to inquire at the residence of his father, Wei Ting Rong. According to him, Yuan Sheng went to Hangzhou and would return in about a week. After this search, the result was that Yuan Sheng,

although not captured,

had mostly returned the property Gan Lai stole. Later, Gan Deng Lai claimed that there were still 5,000 coupons and 2,300 yuan in cash, which he gave to Wang Xin Quan to take back to his hometown in Yuyao. So Li and Su immediately went to Yuyao, but they did not find the original stolen goods. They only found a piece of wrapping paper for the coupons, and Wang Xin Quan was not found either. Yesterday morning was the date for the continued trial. The police station still sent Gan Deng Lai to the First Special Court, where Judge Feng Shi De interrogated him. Jiang Bao Lian, the lawyer for the police station,

described the process.

After the condolences, he requested another postponement, stating that Wei Yuan Sheng and Wang Xin Quan, the important criminals, had not yet been arrested and the case could not proceed. On the other hand, the detectives were stepping up their efforts to arrest them. Jin Yu Securities hired lawyer Wu Lin Kun as its representative and filed an incidental civil lawsuit against Gan Deng Lai, stating that in addition to the actual embezzlement, the defendant also caused damages of (1) treasury bills with a face value of 5,000 yuan, (2) 1,986.71 yuan in cash, and (3) 473.50 yuan in interest coupons, and (4) 2,834.85 yuan in damages for private transactions. The plaintiff requested a judgment ordering the defendant to repay the money. The defendant also hired lawyer Jiang Yi Ping to defend him. As a result, the court ordered the defendant to be detained and the hearing to be postponed for seven days.

Success in Salvaging the Maoli No. 2 Vessel

First Step is to Seal the Hatches; Pumping Water to Float Vessel to Begin Today

The Maoli No. 2 vessel of the Maoli Shipping Bureau sank just after docking at Dinghai on its maiden voyage from Shanghai on July 11. Subsequently, the China Marine Insurance Association entrusted the British firm Lai Si Yanghang to send technicians and workers to Dinghai for salvage. Since construction began, it has been more than half a month. Yesterday, this port received a telegram from the technicians salvaging the vessel, reporting that divers had been sent into the water and all hatch doors had been sealed on the 7th of this month. The first step of the work was completed. It was originally planned to start pumping water on the 8th, but due to the excessive wind and waves, it was changed to starting pumping water on the 10th. Once the accumulated water inside the ship is pumped out, it will float to the surface and be towed back to Shanghai.

Maid Commits Suicide for Love; Follows Chauffeur in Death; Master Unjustly Implicated

Su Xing Hua, a Cantonese girl, is seventeen years old this year. She is slender and lovely. She lost her parents at a young age and was sold to Chen Wu Min (formerly the commander of the First Army of the Five Provinces剿匪 Army in Hunan, Hubei, Jiangsu, Anhui, and Jiangxi) as a maid at the age of seven. She received a superficial education. The Chen family resides at 15 Enlihe Road in the French Concession and owns a private car, hiring Wang Lian Bao (25 years old this year) from Kunshan as a chauffeur. Wang is a handsome young man. Although he is a chauffeur, his clothes in his spare time are like those of a rich man. Xing Hua and Wang serve in the same family. The girl's love for the first time, and the two secretly fell in love. Both parties have the intention of getting married, but their master does not know it. Because the two found it difficult to open their mouths to their master to ask, they did not get their wish. Xing Hua secretly went out at the beginning of last month, intending to marry Wang permanently. Therefore, she lingered in Wang's handyman's home. Because the master's search was urgent, the girl returned home. However, her master suspected that Wang Lian Bao had seduced her, and the mistress was cold to Wang. She hired another car to travel every day and refused to hire Wang. After being stimulated, Wang committed suicide by poisoning himself in the master's car room on the 6th of last month. The suicide note involved Xing Hua's private escape and the master's cold treatment. On the next day, Chen's servant Yu Fu discovered that Wang was dead, reported it to the police station, and sent the body car to the morgue for an autopsy. The Special Second Court sent personnel to inspect the body, and the family collected the body. Chen's family did not live in the house after Wang's death due to superstition and opened a room at the Cangzhou Hotel on Jing'an Temple Road. Xing Hua also followed her master. However, since Wang Lian Bao's death, she had been depressed and unhappy. Recently, she had suicidal thoughts. On the 7th, she went out without her master's permission to buy new shoes and socks and two boxes of raw opium (one yuan per box). At 9 pm, she went to Renhe Hotel at 114 Fada Road, East Zilaihuo Street, French Concession, under the pseudonym Zheng Yong Chang, falsely reporting that she was 20 years old, and opened room number 4 to check in. She committed suicide by poisoning herself. After taking the poison, she changed her clothes, shoes and socks, decorated and applied powder, and lay down waiting for death to come. At 0:30 pm on the 8th, tea room waiter Wang Jinyuan (19 years old, from Pudong) saw that she had not gotten up yet, so he knocked on the door. He called for a long time but there was no response. When he opened the door and went inside to check, he found that she had already died. The body was cold, so he reported it to the French police station. Detectives were sent to investigate and found two suicide notes, stating the death of Lian Bao, etc., and stating the address of her master. The body was carried to the Tongren Fuyuan Branch Hall autopsy room. Her master was notified. Yesterday, the Special Second Court was requested. Prosecutor Wang, accompanied by a forensic scribe, etc., came to the institute for an autopsy. The master sent his servant Yu Fu to the case to represent the collection of the body. The official questioned tea room waiter Wang Jinyuan and Yu Fu and reviewed the deceased's suicide notes. The official declared that Su Xing Hua, Zheng Yong Chang, had indeed committed suicide by poisoning while alive. The body was handed over to Yu Fu for collection and his master was notified to inform the family of the body.

Regulations of the Ministry of Railways: Standardizing Names for Pickled Eggs, Yesterday's Order to Two Railway Bureaus to Comply

The two railway administrations, yesterday received an order from the Ministry of Railways, according to a case presented by the Business Department, regarding an inquiry from the Jiaoji Railway Management Committee about whether a product called "Songhua" (pine flower egg), also known as "Biandan" (preserved egg), should be categorized under which item. After checking the Ministry's Commodity Classification Table, Category 5 of the Livestock Section, there is an item for "pickled eggs" (refer to 26), which should include all kinds of pickled eggs such as Songhua. However, Category 6 of the Industry Section lists "pickled eggs" as third class. Since the names in these two items are inconsistent, the Industry Section 6 should change its name to "pickled eggs," following the name listed in Agriculture Section 5, to ensure uniformity, and still classify it as third class. As for the names Songhua or Biandan, they should not be listed separately in the Ministry's Commodity Classification Table. Based on the presented situation, a general order is issued to all railways to comply. Besides separate orders, this is the order. The bureau has already instructed the transportation department to comply.

Kidnappers from Wujiang Arrested in Shanghai

Ling Yuanpei, the district chief of the Sixth District of Wujiang County, Suzhou, recently received a tip from informants that three bandits from Wujiang, Lu Songlin, Lu Qiulin, and Lu Asan, who had repeatedly committed kidnapping and robbery in the district, were hiding at No. 1 Sanqing Lane, Baille Road, in the French Concession of Shanghai. Ling immediately reported to the Wujiang County Magistrate Xu Youchuan, who prepared a document and sent Ling to Shanghai. At 5 AM yesterday, Ling reported to the French Police and requested assistance in apprehending and transferring them. The police chief then dispatched detectives Bu Zhenglong, Xu Jinlong, and Liu Deyi to go to the address at 8 AM. First, at No. 1 Sanqing Lane, they arrested Lu A'er (38 years old, from Wujiang) and Chen Genlin (45 years old, from Suzhou). Then, at No. 12 of the same lane, they arrested Wu Zaiying (24 years old, from Wujiang), Lu Songlin (39 years old, from Wujiang), Wang Genfu (25 years old, from Suzhou), and Gao Jinsheng (30 years old, from Suzhou). They were taken to the police station and, at 11 AM, escorted to the Second Special Court, where Criminal Court President Wang Gangxu interrogated them in Criminal Court One. Attorney Yuan Jiahong from the Police Department presented the case, stating that the Wujiang County Government had requested the Police Department's assistance in arresting the defendants, and now Wujiang County had sent personnel to request their transfer. He asked the court to rule on the matter. Then, a representative from Wujiang County described the defendants' crimes. After questioning the defendants about their age, place of origin, and occupation, the court ruled that the defendants would be detained pending the formal written request from the Wujiang County Government before further processing.

Impersonating Court Investigators to Extort Money

Recently, a kind of rogue with a wild idea has emerged, impersonating court investigators to extort investigation fees from litigants. Quite a few people have fallen victim. Last month, in the case of Gu Jinlin, a young woman residing in Zhabei, who hired lawyer Pan Zhensheng to sue her husband, Wang Shou'an, for divorce in the local court, before the verdict was delivered, a man wearing a suit and glasses suddenly came to Gu Jinlin's house, claiming to be an investigator from the court and demanding an investigation fee of seven yuan and fifty cents, saying that he had also received the fee from Wang Shou'an's family. Gu Jinlin, being a woman, did not suspect anything and, lacking the money, borrowed it from her uncle, Mr. Gu. Her uncle, upon hearing this, found it strange, as the court never had the title of "investigator." He asked the man whether he had any official investigation documents. The man replied that he did not. He then asked if he had any court identification. The man replied that he did not bring it. Thus, it was proven that he was impersonating someone to commit fraud. He was immediately seized, and just as they were about to call the police, the man was completely embarrassed, his face flushed, and he repeatedly kowtowed and begged for mercy. As a result, Mr. Gu slapped him, and his glasses were knocked to the ground and shattered. The man fled in disgrace, and all the onlookers applauded with delight.

Robbery in Lujiadu Last Night

No. 177, Lan Tang (Garbage Pond), Bin Nan, Lujiadu, Pudong, has been the residence of Wang Asan from Taizhou, a garbage headman. In recent years, due to the booming business, he also runs a small gang of workers who unload foreign pine at various lumberyards. He has accumulated some savings, which has attracted the attention of bandits. At 7:45 PM last night, just as the heavy rain had stopped, Wang was sipping tea in a small teahouse nearby when two unfamiliar men came up to him and called him outside, claiming they wanted to go to Wang's house to discuss something. Unexpectedly, when Wang returned home, there were already three or four people standing at the door. They pushed him inside, displayed a handgun, and forbade him from making a sound. The bandits then rummaged through the chests and cabinets, robbing gold jewelry and silver dollars worth about two hundred yuan, and fled north. Before leaving, they fired two shots into the sky as a warning. One of the bandits dropped his straw hat on the ground due to the wind. As he bent down to pick it up, Mr. Zhang, who was enjoying the cool air, caught a glimpse of him, grabbed him, and handed him over to the police officer on duty, who took him to the Yangjiadu Police Station. That night, Director Yang summoned the victim, who confirmed the man's identity without error. According to the bandit, his name is Qiu Lizheng, 33 years old, from Shandong, with no fixed address. He also said that there was an accomplice named Zhang Yatu, who was hiding at No. 520 Xin Street, Dama Road, Nanshi. Yesterday morning, detectives Zhang Yanbiao and Cheng Peizhang were dispatched to arrest him, but he had already fled. The suspect Wang Yulin was taken to the station for detention and transferred to the General Bureau for questioning.

Sentences for Those Illegally Selling Red Pills

Detectives Wang Rusong, Mao Jinsheng, and Bao Detective Wang Dongwan and Guo Shao etc. of the French Concession Police, at 8 AM on the 20th of last month, cracked down on a red pill trafficking operation at No. 245 Huage'er Road, Zao Bi Jian (cooking stove room), arresting Dai Zhao from Taizhou (23 years old) and Zheng Jinquan (16 years old), seizing 5,000 red pills packed in five bags and two Huaye Bank checkbooks, and taking them to the police station. They confessed that the manufacturing location was in the pavilion room on the second floor of No. 14 Dexing Lane, West Xinqiao Street. The detectives immediately went to the address to search, but the main offender had fled upon hearing the news. They only seized eight bags of red pills, totaling 4,000 pills, plus 6,250 loose pills, a bundle of Tie Guai Li (Iron Crutch Li) trademark paper, and manufacturing raw materials and equipment, and sent them to the Second Special Court. The Police Department's lawyer filed a public prosecution in accordance with Article 6 of the Anti-Opium Law. The details have been reported in previous news. The case has been tried and concluded by President Wang Gangxu of the Second Special Court. Yesterday morning at 9 AM, President Wang presided over Criminal Court One and ordered the two offenders to be brought to court, sentencing Dai Xukai to one year and four months of imprisonment and Zheng Jinquan to one year and eight months of imprisonment. The seized red pills and other items were confiscated. During the appeal period, the defendants were transferred back to the detention center.

Shops and all residents along the streets inside and outside Dunheli, Ladu Road, French Concession, due to the sluggish market, weak business, high rents, and unbearable burden, have united to organize the "Dunheli Branch of the 8th District Branch of the Shanghai Second Special Zone Citizens' Union" and have been approved by the Shanghai Second Special Zone Citizens' Union to organize and send personnel to guide them. Anyone who violates this will be considered a public enemy. (5) Send another letter to the Taylor Company to make a final request for rent reduction. (6) Branch address. Resolved: Affix it to the 8th District Branch, and the staff will discuss the use of it with the society to facilitate matters. The meeting was adjourned.

Registration of the Sanhe Pickled Vegetable Full Image Trademark

The various products of the Yangzhou Sanhe Pickled Vegetable Company, sold by the Jihuatang Pharmacy at the northern end of West Xinqiao, are widely sold due to their exquisite craftsmanship and unique taste. The Trademark Bureau has examined and approved it as legal and issued Registration Certificate No. 26471, stating that the company has obtained the exclusive right to use the Sanhe and full image trademarks from May 15th of this year. Ministry of Education Order: Improvement of Private Universities and Colleges in Peiping and Tianjin

The Ministry of Education issued the following order on the 9th to private universities and colleges in Peiping and Tianjin, urging them to earnestly improve:

Fu Jen University

The order to Fu Jen Catholic University stated, "The school has been previously instructed by the Ministry to improve based on key points. According to the report of the inspectors this time, the research work of various departments in the College of Science and the Department of Chinese Literature in the College of Liberal Arts is commendable. However, there has been little improvement on the points mentioned in the Ministry's order. Therefore, the following are specifically listed, and compliance is required: 1. The school has limited funding and too many departments, making it difficult to achieve balanced development. The departments of Philosophy, Psychology, Education, and Social Economics should be promptly considered for consolidation and reported to the Ministry for approval. The teaching staff and equipment of the Art Specialization Program need to be supplemented. The curriculum outlines of each department should be promptly formulated and effectively implemented. 2. The school's teachers still consist mostly of part-time staff. Efforts should be made to increase the number of full-time staff and limit outside teaching. The research and investigation work of the Department of Chinese Literature must have the participation of domestic personnel and should cooperate with local national academic institutions to achieve greater results in the work. Therefore, you are ordered to earnestly improve and report accordingly."

Yenching University

The order to Yenching University stated, "The school has been previously instructed by the Ministry to improve based on key points. According to the report of the inspectors this time, the school has made considerable improvements on the points mentioned in the Ministry's order. The research work of the Biology Department is particularly commendable. However, the departments established by the school are still too numerous and should be further consolidated. The pre-medical and pre-nursing departments have not yet been discontinued, which is inappropriate. These departments must be terminated this year. The school's endowment should be actively raised to solidify its foundation. The extravagant habits of students still need to be corrected. Therefore, you are ordered to earnestly improve and report accordingly."

Nankai University

The order to Nankai University stated, "The school has been previously instructed by the Ministry to improve based on key points. According to the report of the inspectors this time, the school has generally paid attention to the points mentioned in the previous order, and there has been progress in other areas compared to before. However, the teaching staff of the Physics Department still needs to be strengthened, and the amount of equipment funds should also be increased. Therefore, you are ordered to comply with the improvement. This order."

Sino-French University

The order to Sino-French University stated, "The school has been previously instructed by the Ministry to improve based on key points. According to the report of the inspectors, the school has added 40,000 yuan worth of books and instruments in the past year, and the research work of the Physics and Chemistry Departments in the College of Science has achieved excellent results, all of which are commendable. The previous order to abolish the College of Social Sciences has also been complied with. However, there are still points that need to be improved, which are listed below: 1. After the College of Social Sciences was abolished, the original Departments of Philosophy and Social Sciences were assigned to the College of Liberal Arts. However, the students of these two departments are still receiving classes at the original location. The number of students in these two departments is not large, and they should be moved into the College after the summer vacation. The name of the Department of Social Sciences is too general, and the nature of the department should be determined, and the name should be changed accordingly. 2. The number of part-time teachers still accounts for the majority, and should be reduced as much as possible, and excellent full-time teachers should be hired. For teachers taking leave, strict make-up class measures should be established. 3. The equipment of the electromagnetics and wireless electricity laboratories should be strengthened, and important reference books and complete sets of journals for each department of the College of Science should also be added. Therefore, you are ordered to comply with and report accordingly."

Chaoyang College

The order to Chaoyang College stated, "The school has been previously instructed by the Ministry to improve based on key points. According to the report of the inspectors this time, the school has only made improvements in accounting and has added some books.

Plan for Implementing Compulsory Education (Middle) (Lei Zhen's Broadcast Speech on the Central Radio Station)

4. Funding

The funding for compulsory education is primarily the responsibility of the local authorities. In urban areas, it is coordinated by the municipal government, and in counties and cities within provinces, it is shared by the provincial and county governments in appropriate proportions. The central government may provide subsidies based on the conditions of the provinces and cities. As for remote and impoverished provinces, where fundraising is too difficult, the central government may provide special subsidies to ensure the widespread and smooth progress of compulsory education.

Now that the implementation of compulsory education has begun, various provinces are actively proceeding. According to the implementation plans reported by various provinces and cities, approximately 18 million yuan or more is required. The provinces plan to raise 9 million yuan themselves, which is far from enough. In addition to the 2.4 million yuan from the national treasury that can be used for subsidies, there is also 500,000 yuan for border education expenses and 800,000 yuan from the Boxer Indemnity allocated to compulsory education, which are also being considered for distribution. The numbers proposed by each province and city, the amounts they plan to raise themselves, and the amounts subsidized by the central government are reported separately below.

List of Expenses for Implementing Compulsory Education in Various Provinces (Omitted)

Other shortcomings have not been effectively improved. I will remind you again, and you must strictly abide by them, and report back for record. (4) The college's entrance examinations should strictly set admission standards, and would rather have vacancies than to admit unqualified students. Regular assessments must also be strictly distinguished in order to improve quality and increase the level of performance. (5) Among the college's seventy-one teachers, fifty-two of them have monthly salaries below one hundred yuan, which shows that there are many part-time teachers. In the future, the treatment should be increased appropriately, and the number of part-time staff should be reduced, and full-time teachers should be hired. (6) The college's dormitory kitchens and various sanitary facilities are very unclean and should be improved as soon as possible. This order."

Ming Kuo College

The order to Ming Kuo College stated, "The college has previously been prompted by this Ministry regarding the key points of improvement and has been ordered to comply with them and register them. Based on the reports of the inspectors this time, the college is considered to be serious in training and managing students, and the library equipment has also been slightly increased. However, the points of hiring full-time professors, increasing treatment, adding various equipment, improving student level, and enriching the content of disciplines have not been effectively improved, and the previous order should still be strictly followed. In addition, the endowment should be increased, the accounting system should be improved quickly, the office expenses should be reduced as much as possible within the expenditure budget, and the book expenses should be increased, and important college affairs should be discussed and decided by the college affairs conference. You are therefore ordered to earnestly comply and report back."

Issuing a Declaration

The Association, in order to promote children's welfare and arouse the attention of all sectors for Children's Year, hereby issues the following declaration: The nationally designated Children's Year has opened amidst cheers and celebrations across the country on August 1st. Observing the grand ceremonies held in various places and the enthusiastic donations, we are sincerely fortunate, which is enough to symbolize the importance that the people of the country attach to children's welfare. However, the significance of the establishment of Children's Year is by no means limited to the acquisition of this grand ceremony. The holding of the opening ceremony is only sufficient to express the nation's emphasis on the founding of children and its determination to work hard, and the tree of actual achievements still depends on future efforts. Otherwise, the establishment of Children's Year is no different from formal embellishment. What is the value of this move? Since the central government decided to implement the nationally designated Children's Year, in addition to the joint organization of the National Children's Year Implementation Committee by various departments to plan everything, the provincial and municipal governments have also organized local Children's Year Implementation Committees as the hub for promoting children's welfare undertakings. Not only is the organization strict and the system clear, but the preparations before the event have also undergone a long period of planning. Even in this city, the implementation committee has been established for a long time and has held many meetings. Although no specific plan has been promulgated yet and no actual projects have been held, the future will surely be gratifying to us. However, the construction of children's welfare undertakings is complicated. In order to promote and develop, in addition to the advocacy of the government, the entire people must concentrate their efforts and jointly assist. It is hoped that the crowd will easily accomplish it and the results can be seen. This city is the only major commercial port in our country, and it is also an area where humanities gather. The concept of cherishing children has not yet penetrated every citizen, but the perception of all sectors of society should not lack wise men. If we can all rise up to assist the existing children's welfare national system, earnestly seek to increase children's welfare, and give it practical support, then the future of children's undertakings in this city will undoubtedly be able to achieve greater achievements. Our Association, as one of the children's welfare organizations in this city, has exhausted its meager efforts to promote the establishment of Children's Year, and has even deeper hopes after the establishment of Children's Year. Therefore, in addition to suggesting that the Municipal Children's Year Implementation Committee expedite the holding of actual projects, we sincerely hope that all sectors of the city will do their best to jointly seek the promotion of children's welfare and complete the mission of Children's Year. This Association dares to speak for the children of the whole city. This is a declaration to be reviewed.

Little Men (10)

—Original by American author Louisa May Alcott, translated by Zheng Xiaocang (Zonghai)

Their conversation had reached Mrs. Bhaer's ears, but she seemed to be only concentrating on pouring milk and taking care of little Tandy. At that time, poor Serba was already drowsy. He had already put his spoon to his eyes, nodding like a poppy in the wind. Finally, he leaned his cheek on a piece of soft bread and fell sound asleep. The reason why Mrs. Bhaer placed Nat next to Tommy was because the fat, short boy was amiable and easygoing, so shy people liked to be close to him. Nat also felt this, and during dinner, he said a few heartfelt words to him, which seemed to give Mrs. Bhaer a way to know the boy's character, which was far better than talking to him herself.

In Mr. Lawrance's letter of introduction for Nat, he wrote:

Dear Mrs. Bhaer,——Here is something that suits your heart. This poor boy is now an orphan, poor and helpless. He has been playing music on the street to make a living. I found him in a cellar, mourning his deceased father and his lost violin. I think he can be made to do something, so I thought we could give this little one a helping hand. You heal his tired body, and Fritz helps his wasted mind. After he succeeds, let me see if he is a genius or just has some talent, and he can have a skill to avoid freezing and starving. Give him a chance, if only for your own boy, 'Tandy.'"

Mrs. Bhaer read the letter and exclaimed, "Of course we are willing"! When she saw Nat, she immediately felt that whether he was a genius or not, what he needed was a child with poverty and sickness, and what he needed was her willing, to be a family and a mother's general protection. She and Mr. Bhaer were secretly observing him. They felt that although he was wearing ragged clothes, had a dirty face, and acted unnaturally, he had many lovable qualities. He was a twelve-year-old boy with a pale, thin face and blue eyes. Under his loose, unkempt hair, he had a broad forehead. His face sometimes showed a look of anxiety, as if he was about to be scolded or beaten. His lips were very sensitive. When someone treated him with kindness, he would smile slightly. Gentle words immediately caused a look of gratitude, which made people very lovable. When Tommy mentioned the music team, Mrs. Bhaer immediately saw that eager and happy expression on his face, and she said to herself, "This poor little darling, if he likes it, he can play the violin all day long."

Arrived in Shanghai Yesterday and Scheduled to Depart by Ship on the 13th; Accompanied by Four National Martial Arts Institute Advisors

(Shanghai Times Agency Report) Zhang Zhijiang, member of the Central Committee and Director of the Central National Martial Arts Institute, arrived in Shanghai from Nanjing yesterday to prepare for his trip. He is scheduled to depart on the President Coolidge on the 13th of this month.

Study Physical Education Abroad

According to Mr. Zhang, he has always believed that the strength of a nation depends primarily on the physical fitness of its people. Therefore, the promotion of national martial arts and physical education in our country is essential for rescuing our national crisis. In particular, national martial arts are a skill in which our country excels, and there is a need to promote and develop them. He had previously resolved to travel abroad to promote Chinese martial arts internationally and to study the actual conditions of physical education in Europe and America, hoping to learn from their strengths and make up for our shortcomings so that our country's physical education and national martial arts can be improved.

Performing Martial Arts in Europe, America, and Southeast Asia

He is scheduled to depart on the President Coolidge on the 13th of this month, bound for America. His entourage includes Mr. Luo Jiezhi and Peng Shu, advisors to the National Martial Arts Institute; Luo Guanghai, staff member of the Overseas Department of the Central Party Headquarters; and Shi Yufang, a pastor from the Presbyterian Church. The trip is expected to last six months, but may be slightly extended if necessary. After arriving in America, he will travel to various European countries, including England, Germany, and France. On his way back to China, he plans to make some stops in Southeast Asia. During his travels in Europe and America, he plans to perform national martial arts at any time so that people in Europe and America can understand the true meaning of Chinese martial arts. When he arrives in Southeast Asia, he will telegraph back to China to organize national martial arts and basketball teams to participate in joint performances.

Spring and Autumn

Snippets

— (Microorganism)

An extremely weak melon vine can bear a "bucket-sized" watermelon, unafraid of wind and rain. A tall ginkgo tree, on the other hand, bears only tiny white fruit, which falls off after a single night of wind and rain. This is just like how wealthy families often have few children, while families with difficult lives often have many.

The commercial field is like a gambling den. When natives buy native goods, it is like family members playing mahjong. The money won and lost still doesn't leave the house. But if natives buy foreign goods, it is as if a few foreigners have joined the game. If we win, that's fine, but if we lose, doesn't the money immediately leave the house? Furthermore, there is still hope of winning at gambling, but this is simply a case of losing without winning, how frightening!

Mysterious Night

— Yan Chonglou

It really is like a play; as soon as the dignified "main character" leaves the stage, the clownish "night" jumps out.

Night, no matter how naturally dark it may be, can be illuminated with the light of electric torches, and sometimes it can even be painted with red, green, blue, purple… all sorts of different colors. Women whose faces look withered and yellow in the daytime become very beautiful at night; members of the privileged class who spend their days listlessly in bed (note… "gun" here refers to an opium pipe) become full of energy at night; the taverns and teahouses are filled with moralistic gentlemen who lecture their sons on "abstaining from wine and women"; the dance halls are packed with scholars who have undergone training in the morning – preparing to sacrifice themselves for the country; clerks in foreign firms and shop assistants, dragging their tired bodies after a day of hard work, send their day's wages into the dog racing tracks and jai alai courts without hesitation… these are the various scenes that unfold in the city at night: night can help make faces beautiful, night can help make people full of energy, night can make people change all normal states.

Night, how truly mysterious!

But the light that seems so bright at night becomes dim under the sun; the woman who looks so beautiful at night, like the lamplight, dares not be put under the sun.

Slippers

— Zhou Xian

Slippers, whether worn by the "upper class" or the "lower class," are loved by everyone. Especially during this summer season, after work, one feels that slippers are indispensable.

The uppers of slippers can be very elaborate. White satin embroidered with red flowers and green leaves, and adorned with one or two lifelike black butterflies, is naturally the most beautiful. Of course, slippers with such beautiful uppers, worn on the feet of a young playboy, are most likely to attract attention, and people will ask mysteriously, "Who is the lover who gave you these slippers?"

In recent years, the use of silk thread embroidery on slipper uppers has gradually decreased, and most now use beads. Some are embroidered with cross-stitch, but I feel that it doesn't quite match the richness and elegance of white satin silk embroidery.

However, this year, general shoe stores are displaying large quantities of leather slippers, marked at "one yuan per pair," or even eighty cents per pair. Thus, the beaded and cross-stitched slippers that had overthrown the white satin embroidered slippers have now been defeated. Among ten slipper wearers, regardless of gender, age, wealth, or status, at least eight or nine are wearing leather slippers. Shoe store owners might shout "Long live leather slippers!"

Yesterday, at a certain company, I saw a pair of high-heeled women's slippers, with heels a full inch and a half high. I couldn't help but feel somewhat emotional. I feel that the original purpose of wearing slippers is simply for comfort. To wear slippers with such high heels in the name of comfort, what's the point?

Husband Eating

Goring's Letter

— Ping

The Goring here is not a place name, but a person's name; not the German Goring, but the Chinese Goring. Separating the two characters, Ge refers to Ge Gongzhen, and Lin refers to Lin Yutang. Readers should know: one is a famous reporter, and the other is a famous writer. Their relationship is that of old friends for many years, not just casual acquaintances. Recently, because of a postscript to an article in "Ren Jian Shi" (Human World), "Lin" said a few words that caused "Ge" unhappiness. "Ge" sent a letter from overseas, in which he defends himself to "Lin" with humorous wording. It is specially introduced to readers:

'Mr. Yutang: Long time no see, I often enjoy reading your journals while abroad. I recently read your postscript to "A Reporter's Career" in the 28th issue of "Ren Jian Shi," in which you criticized me. Because it is contrary to the facts, I dare not remain silent. You have been in the publishing industry for a long time, and should know that today's Chinese newspapers do not yet have the world perspective of the *New York Times*, which is willing to spend huge sums of money to select talented people and station them abroad to seek the latest news and information. You have also been in the writing world for a long time, and should also know that today's Chinese magazines are very cautious in their selection of materials and dare not publish articles about Soviet writers. I have tried and failed, and am not exaggerating. Therefore, my trip to the Soviet Union was entirely out of personal interest and was not at someone's behest. I could not seek Duranty's position where he could write the truth as he saw it, and I could not seek a newspaper like Duranty's that could publish whatever he wanted.

Moreover, there are already many books about the Soviet Union in China. Although I am unwilling to write travelogues or translations again, I must personally witness things before I write about them. In recent years, the following articles have been scattered in "Shenghuo Zhoukan" (Life Weekly), "Xinsheng Zhoukan" (New Life Weekly), "Guowen Zhoubao" (National News Weekly), "Shijie Zhishi" (World Knowledge), and "Shidai Huabao" (The China Illustrated Review):

The Second Five-Year Plan, Electric City, Oil City, Iron City, and Charcoal City, The so-called Social City, The Soviet National Day, The Seventh General Election, The Tenth Anniversary of Lenin's Death, Military Parade and Sports Parade, Fifteen Years of Soviet Art.

The above are all the more meaningful ones, and other miscellaneous works are not included. I believe that this is purely my own effort, hoping to contribute to the people of the country. If it were for the sake of earning money, then only two or three yuan per thousand words, you should know it even better. Several months of hard work may not even be enough to pay for a day's travel expenses. "The words of a humble man are insignificant," what is so strange about that? But you edit newspapers without reading them, I cannot but blame you, sir. Gongzhen bows and writes, Vienna, June 29th.'

Small Western Heaven

— Written by Zhang Henshui

Chapter 17: Don't Ask a Daughter's Body Difficult to Speak Hidden Pain Compete to See Noble People Encoffined Together Admire Noble Demeanor

Huanhua nodded and said, "Goodbye." She couldn't care less about where You stood, and turned to go inside. When she got to the backyard, she saw Cheng Zhiqian looking out through the glass window from afar. So she stopped smiling, put on a melancholy face, and went to the room. Zhiqian smiled and said, "Miss Yang is enthusiastic again afterwards, she must have gone there for a turn." Huanhua sighed and said, "Mr. Cheng, you really are a good person, the more I think about your words, the more I regret it. I regret being the matchmaker so much." As she spoke, she pressed her hands on the edge of the table, looking at Zhiqian, as if waiting for Zhiqian's comfort. Zhiqian then smiled and said, "Speaking of which, this matter cannot be blamed on any one person, and moreover, his family was originally willing to do so." As he spoke, he poured a cup of tea and handed it to Huanhua. She smiled and thanked him, and sat down, describing Yueying's appearance in detail, naturally all on the side of sympathy. Later, Zhiqian said that the end of a woman with a weak will was nothing more than this, Huanhua was silent, and then tears flowed down her face. After a long time, she wiped her tears, lowered her head, and said, "If all men had a heart like Mr. Cheng, women could travel all over the world and not be fooled." Zhiqian smiled and said, "Miss Yang said such a thing, I can't take it seriously. But I am a poor scholar, and there is no talk of any enjoyment. I know how to be content with my lot and dare not have any delusions. A person who is content with his lot will naturally not harm women. If I had a hundred thousand or eight hundred thousand, living in a palace-like house and riding in the latest model car, then I would naturally marry three or four concubines." (286)

Records of the Fragrant Imperial Past

— Originally written by Princess Der Ling of the Qing Dynasty, translated by Qin Shouou

They all flew very low, and some almost brushed their wings across the water's surface; in front of us, countless lotus leaves rose and fell to the left and right with the gusts of dawn wind; the tiny waves stirred up by the lake would sometimes submerge them all together, but soon they would struggle back up, swaying so that the water on the leaves would become round dots and fall down, looking like glittering pearls in the not-so-bright morning light.

Everyone was silent, there was no sound anywhere, as silent as in the middle of the desert; the entire Summer Palace, not a single light could be seen, as if it were still asleep. It was really funny that we were all out so early today, as if we were doing something secret. Actually, I really don't understand what the Empress Dowager meant by telling us to get up so early today and follow her to the lake: I don't dare be sure whether others have understood it. But the Empress Dowager's expression was very calm and composed—because she herself already knew what kind of adventure was about to be discovered: I saw that there was indeed some mysterious expression on her face, and it seemed that she was still thinking about something. Her eyes were either looking at that large pile of lotus leaves, or raised to look at the sky to the east.

"Everyone pay attention!" she suddenly said to us in a low voice again: "A rare sight will appear before your eyes! When the sun rises, watch carefully, all the unopened lotus buds will bloom in an instant!" (386)

Character Vignettes

The Nobility of Hitler's Sister

— Special

The world-renowned and globally influential German leader Hitler has a sister who, by common sense, is also a noble person. But she does not think of climbing the social ladder, but stays away from her brother and lives in seclusion in a foreign country. This noble personality is beyond the reach of today's modern wives and misses, and some people may even say that she is eccentric.

This is Ms. Paula Hitler, who is thirty-eight years old this year and still a spinster. She lives in seclusion in Vienna, Austria, and quietly watches her brother display his heroic talents and great plans. She only goes to Germany once a year to visit her brother, and only stays for a few weeks before returning. Hitler once said that if his "doctrine" succeeds and makes his relatives rich and prosperous, that would be an immoral act. Ms. Paula agrees with this very much, and it can truly be said that like brother, like sister.

Ms. Paula often says to her friends: she would be happier than anything else if she could support herself again one day. She used to work in an insurance company writing envelopes, and her monthly salary was very meager, barely enough to live on. Two years ago, she was suddenly fired, and she ran around trying to find a new job, but she couldn't. She deliberately misspelled her name, but eventually people found out that she was the sister of the leader of the National Socialist Party, and she lost her job at the insurance company because of this. Later, no business dared to hire her anymore, so she had to rely on her brother's allowance to live. She was very sad to be dependent on others. Her brother's allowance was about sixty or seventy yuan a month, taken in installments, each time about ten yuan or so.

She originally lived in a small dilapidated house in the heart of the city, which was very uncomfortable. Three months ago, she moved to near the Wahring district, where many residents belong to the National Socialist Party. Through the introduction of a friend, she rented two rooms in a new building, with a separate kitchen and bathroom, which was much more spacious than before.

In addition to paying a monthly rent of fourteen yuan for this new house, she also subsidized the construction cost of five hundred yuan. This sum, and the cost of adding some furniture, were all provided by her brother.

Although she registered using her real name, her neighbors only know her as Mrs. Wolf. The reason why she wanted to hide it from them was because, in the place she used to live, there were often uninvited guests who came to pester her endlessly, so she wanted to avoid this trouble. Later, an indiscreet newspaper published her new address in the newspaper, so many people went to visit her, and she had to take refuge in a friend's house for a week. She has received thousands of letters, some asking her to intercede with her brother's actions, some full of flattery, and some full of abuse, all three types of letters are what she hates.

This sister of the leader who holds the power of Germany, does not hire a servant at home, and takes care of all the housework herself. Sometimes, when a reporter rings the doorbell, they see a woman with simple clothes, a strong physique, tanned hands, and jet-black hair come to answer the door. At a glance, it is known that she is Hitler's sister. She only opens the door a crack, and when the guest asks if Mrs. Wolf is at home, she firmly replies, "Madam is not at home, I don't know when she will be back." When the guest tries to ask another question, the door slams shut.

Ms. Paula loves to live quietly and rarely chats with her neighbors. The only people she usually meets are a few friends, two middle-aged women and a man, who is the one who found her the new house.

Ms. Paula returns to Germany once a year and spends a few weeks with her brother, but she also lives in seclusion. Her whereabouts are never made public. When she lives in Germany, she only spends her time with the wives of her brother's most trusted comrades.

Hitler also has a foster sister named Raba Shuz, who lives in Germany for a long time. She and Ms. Paula never appear in public. This kind of virtue is truly commendable!

Finance News Favorable to Buyers, Gold Bar Premiums Replay a Five Yuan Surge

However, large holders are selling, and the situation has eased.

Yesterday, the gold market rose again after falling. Despite efforts by firms such as Da De Cheng to increase supply, the tight foreign exchange market prevailed. Positive news helped create a situation where demand exceeded supply in the trading floor, causing the price to soar to 918.8 yuan. Eventually, it stabilized. Initially, overseas silver markets saw British prices rise and American prices remain flat. Mont de Piété forward silver prices increased by five hao, and foreign exchange rates rose slightly. London raw gold increased by one penny. Although the market sentiment was initially weak, pre-market trading opened and immediately retreated to 023 yuan, then rose again to 034 yuan. The situation fluctuated. The Central Bank's announced exchange rates showed both British and American prices unchanged, and the customs gold unit also remained the same. The gold bar premium standard price rose to 920.4 yuan, but this had little impact. After opening, selling pressure remained strong, once approaching the 900 yuan mark. Large holders supported the market at the low, and prices soon rebounded. Chinese merchants attempted to purchase US dollars but failed, leading to a surge, but the price did not exceed the 10 yuan mark. Banks released some supply, slightly easing the downstream pressure. However, due to the HSBC exchange rates, both British and American prices remained flat, leading to much struggle after the initial decline. Subsequently, banks scrambled to settle their positions, and the foreign exchange market tightened, pushing the price above the 10 yuan mark. Despite much fluctuation, large holders continued to buy, further tightening the domestic foreign exchange market, and igniting buying interest in the trading floor, once pushing the price to 916 yuan. Banks took advantage of the high prices to release supply, and sellers became active, gradually pushing the price down. There was much contention along the way, but eventually, market sentiment weakened slightly, and predictions of a one anna increase in Indian silver led to a retreat within the 10 yuan mark. Large holders also released supply, and the market weakened at noon. The afternoon market opened flat, and although there was political news, it was unrelated to the gold market. Therefore, the market opened peacefully, and buyers, after a period of inactivity, became active, pushing the price back above the 10 yuan mark, restoring prosperity. The first telegraphic report from Indian silver showed an increase of two annas, but there was still a possibility of reversal. Overall, although the day's trend resulted in an increase, large holders sold off a significant amount, and the situation on the trading floor has eased, making a retreat easier. After Careful Transactions, the Flow of Silver Dollars is Particularly Difficult

This year, due to the decline of rural areas and the withering of urban areas in the Shanghai market, a consistent and cautious approach has been adopted, refusing to lend excessively, resulting in various obstacles and the impact of financial stagnation for all Shanghai merchants. Recently, the market has again suffered from floods and natural disasters in various places, with man-made disasters following closely behind, making it difficult for the market to recover. Therefore, currently, banks are only slightly accommodating to old customers, while other ordinary customers are largely restricted and not provided loans. Cash shops, regardless of new or old customers, are adopting a contractionary approach, making the market even more unbearable and the flow of funds particularly difficult. As a result, there is consistently no competition for interbank loaning of silver dollars in the market. The market price of two jiao every morning and afternoon has remained for more than a month. Yesterday also followed the old pattern, with no added interest and no activity. Although there was some slight fluctuation in the Small Exchange Association, it was only a few fen up or down. The volume of interbank loaning of silver dollar notes was similar to the previous few days, with over 3.2 million transferred in the morning market, over 200,000 in new transactions, and over 200,000 in transactions in the afternoon market. Transactions in the Small Exchange Association were 300,000 to 400,000, with over 500,000 banknotes recovered, 700,000 in circulating notes issued, 800,000 in secret marked notes, 400,000 in silver dollar collateral transactions redeemed, 500,000 in new loans made, 150,000 in inbound and outbound passenger loans, 45 million in public silver dollar bills received and settled by cash shops, 5.2 million in silver dollar interbank loans received and settled, 500,000 in various remittances, and 300,000 to 400,000 in cash received. Additionally, Japanese banks had an inflow of funds of approximately several million, but the exact amount is unknown. However, after checking the Japanese banks' settlements, it was not included, suggesting that there was another type of settlement not included. Foreign banks received and settled 1.7 to 1.8 million in bill payments, 3.0 million in various goods, remittances, collateral, and miscellaneous payments, 500,000 in telegraphic transfers, 500,000 in foreign exchange settlement payments, 800,000 in re-remittances, and 400,000 in warehouse entries. Given the current state of the city, silver money businesses are unwilling to relax, and the situation is expected to become tighter day by day.

Recently, due to the tight money supply and difficulty in circulation, there has been little enthusiasm for transactions of subsidiary coins.
